‚óŹ Excellent ‚ÄĒ the open-design architecture is a near-perfect template to mirror
  (Electron + Next.js shell, a single privileged local daemon that spawns the
  agent CLI as a child process, DESIGN.md brand-system files, SKILL.md skills, a
  plugin marketplace with manifests, an MCP stdio server, BYOK proxy with SSRF
  guards, sandboxed iframe preview, pnpm monorepo). Combined with everything in
  summary.txt (the proven FFmpeg/Whisper/Remotion reel pipeline, including the
  real-world Windows pain points), I have strong grounding.

  Before I write the blueprint, four foundational decisions will materially
  shape the architecture and roadmap. Let me lock these with you.

‚óŹ¬†User declined to answer questions
  ‚éŅ ¬†¬∑ What desktop shell / runtime should the platform be built on? This is 
     foundational ‚ÄĒ it shapes packaging, the installer agent, IPC, and how 
     closely we can mirror open-design. (Electron + Next.js / Tauri + Rust core 
     / Web + local daemon only)
     ¬∑ How should the AI agent layer be powered? You previously framed this as 
     'connected with the Claude CLI.' (Wrap the Claude Code CLI / Anthropic 
     Agent SDK / API / Agent-agnostic (any CLI))
     ¬∑ What should the v1 flagship workflow be? The PRD will document the full 
     grand vision regardless ‚ÄĒ this decides what the realistic first shippable 
     slice optimizes for. (Short-form vertical reels / General NLE depth /

‚óŹ Of course ‚ÄĒ let's talk it through before I lock anything in. These four
  decisions shape the whole blueprint, so it's worth getting them right.

  Here's a quick plain-English version of what each question is really asking,
  so you can tell me where you want to dig in:

  1. Desktop shell ‚ÄĒ What is the app actually built on? Electron is exactly what
  your reference repo (open-design) uses and what VS Code / Cursor use, so it's
  the "copy the proven thing" choice. Tauri is the lighter/faster modern
  alternative but diverges from open-design and is fiddlier on Windows. Web-only
  is the quickest to boot but has no real native app feel.
  2. Agent backbone ‚ÄĒ What's the "brain" wiring? Option 1: the app literally
  launches the Claude Code CLI behind the scenes (what you already use; reuses
  skills, MCP, plan mode, the usage meter). Option 2: we build our own
  multi-agent controller directly on the Claude API (more power, much more to
  build). Option 3: support any agent CLI (Claude/Codex/Cursor‚Ä¶) like
  open-design does.
  3. v1 scope ‚ÄĒ What does the first real version actually do well? The PRD will
  still describe the full grand vision either way; this only decides what the
  first shippable slice nails first. Reels-first = productionize the exact thing
  we already made. NLE-depth = aim at full Premiere-style editing immediately.
  Cockpit-first = ship the beautiful Claude-Code-like shell, video plugs in
  after.
  4. Platform ‚ÄĒ Which OS first? Windows-first matches your laptop and everything
  we've already built and debugged. Cross-platform day one is cleaner long-term
  but a lot more installer work up front.

  So ‚ÄĒ what would you like to clarify? For example:
  - Are any of these terms (Electron vs Tauri, CLI vs SDK, NLE) unclear and you
  want me to explain trade-offs deeper?
  - Do you already have a leaning on any of them and want my honest take on
  whether it's right?
  - Is there a fifth decision you're weighing that I haven't surfaced (e.g.
  local-first vs cloud rendering, free/open-source vs paid, product name)?
  - Or do you want me to just recommend the strongest default for all four and
  explain my reasoning, so you can approve or veto?

  Tell me which ones you want to go deeper on (or "explain all four"), and I'll
  break them down before we decide.

‚óŹ Research done. Two authoritative anchors now ground the design:

  1. open-design's architecture is a near-perfect template ‚ÄĒ Electron + Next.js
  shell, one privileged local daemon (Express + SSE) that spawns the agent CLI
  as a child process in isolated project dirs, DESIGN.md brand-system files,
  SKILL.md skills, a plugin marketplace with manifests, a stdio MCP server, BYOK
  proxy with SSRF guards, sandboxed iframe preview, pnpm monorepo. This maps
  cleanly onto a video tool (swap HTML-artifact streaming for a Video-AST ‚Üí
  render compiler; swap DESIGN.md for a STYLE.md look/brand system).

  2. The Claude CLI is a viable, robust agent backbone. It runs headless (claude
  -p "‚Ä¶" --output-format stream-json --input-format stream-json), streams
  structured JSON events (thinking, tool calls, results, usage), resumes
  sessions (--resume/--session-id), registers MCP servers, supports subagents +
  skills + hooks + permission modes ‚ÄĒ and critically, spawning the CLI reuses
  your existing Claude Pro subscription auth (the Agent SDK via API key would
  bill per-token instead). Models in play: claude-opus-4-8 (default),
  claude-sonnet-4-6, claude-haiku-4-5 for cheap subagents; effort low‚Üímax;
  adaptive thinking.

  So the agent backbone is settled per your steer: the Claude CLI. "User can
  choose" = the in-app control surface picks the model + effort + plan/auto mode
  that get passed to the CLI. "Auto pre-install" = the Installation Agent.

  the entire proof-of-concept, including the Windows-specific issues already

     was scoped to the PRD).

     Architecture spine to be documented (the recommended design)

     Local-first, open-source. Every edit is structured data before it renders ‚ÄĒ
     a versioned
     Video AST / "Edit Decision Document" (EDD, JSON) that is explainable,
     reproducible, inspectable,
     diff-able. Intent ‚Üí Plan ‚Üí EDD ‚Üí IR ‚Üí Execution DAG ‚Üí render.

     Layers:
     1. Cockpit (Electron renderer, Next.js/React): chat pane ¬∑ "alive"
     streaming terminal ¬∑
     control surface (model Opus/Sonnet/Haiku ¬∑ effort low‚Üímax ¬∑ plan/auto mode
     ¬∑ permissions) ¬∑
     usage/limit meter ¬∑ drag-drop media ¬∑ Remotion preview in a sandboxed 
     iframe (open-design pattern).
     2. Daemon (single privileged Node process): the only privileged process.
     Session manager,
     render queue + background workers, OpenVideo MCP server (stdio), BYOK/proxy
     with SSRF guard,
     project workspace/file ops, spawns the Claude CLI +
     ffmpeg/whisper/yt-dlp/remotion as children;
     streams to the renderer over SSE.
     3. Agent layer (Claude CLI, headless): a Director/orchestrator plus
     specialized subagents
     (Planner, Research, Transcript, Audio, Caption, Motion/Animation, B-roll,
     Color, Story/Retention/Hook,
     Music/SFX, QA/Critique, Simulation, Export‚Ä¶) defined as Claude Code
     subagents + skills; tools
     exposed through the MCP server wrapping
     ffmpeg/ffprobe/whisper/remotion/yt-dlp. Each agent doc
     specifies responsibilities ¬∑ inputs ¬∑ outputs ¬∑ memory ¬∑ tools ¬∑
     permissions ¬∑ comms protocol ¬∑
     failure/retry ¬∑ delegation ¬∑ context-window strategy ¬∑ reasoning strategy.
     4. Video engine + compiler: Intent Understanding ‚Üí Planning ‚Üí EDD (Video
     AST) ‚Üí typed IR ‚Üí
     compiler passes (lint, validate, optimize, schedule) ‚Üí Execution DAG.
     Incremental + content-addressed
     cache (asset hashing). Scene graph, motion graph, caption/word-level timing
     model.
     5. Rendering engine: Remotion (React ‚Üí graphics/captions/overlays)
     composited with FFmpeg
     (cut/grade/audio/encode). Documents the proven PoC path (overlay
     PNG-sequence + ffmpeg composite,
     incl. the broken-Remotion-compositor workaround) as the reliable fallback.
     GPU (NVENC/CUDA) with
     CPU fallback; proxy generation; preview vs final; HLG/HDR‚ÜíSDR tonemap;
     codecs/compression; IG/9:16 export.
     6. Installation Agent (tiered): HW detection (GPU/RAM/CPU/disk),
     winget/choco on Windows, PATH repair,
     verify/repair/rollback, progress reporting. The "superpowers before
     editing" layer.
     7. Workspace + version control: per-project tree (projects/ assets/ 
     renders/ cache/ plans/ transcripts/ timelines/ agents/ prompts/ memory/ 
     plugins/ models/ downloads/ exports/ versions/ backups/ logs/), each
     folder's purpose documented; git-backed EDD history = reproducible edits.
     8. Plugin system: open-design-style manifest (openvideo.json) for caption
     styles, transitions,
     templates, animation packs, custom agents/skills, custom renderers,
     music/SFX providers, cloud rendering.
     9. Security: daemon = sole privileged process; tool sandboxing; permission
     model mirroring Claude
     Code permission modes; encrypted secrets/keystore; SSRF-guarded proxy;
     per-project filesystem +
     network permissions; safe-by-default destructive-op confirmation.

       628 + The cockpit never touches the filesystem, spawns a process, 
           +or makes a network call directly.                            
       629 + It speaks only to the daemon. The Claude CLI reasons and cal
           +ls tools (via MCP) but does not                              
       630 + itself encode the product's privileged logic. Deterministic 
           +tools do the heavy media work.                               
       631 +                                                             
       632 + 8.2  The Cockpit (presentation plane)                       
       633 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       634 +   Stack: Electron (Chromium + Node 24) shell hosting a Next.
           +js / React renderer. The renderer                            
       635 +   runs sandboxed (contextIsolation on, nodeIntegration off);
           + all privileged actions go through a                         
       636 +   typed preload bridge to the daemon.                       
       637 +   Responsibilities:                                         
       638 +     - Render the chat, the live "alive" terminal, the contro
           +l surface, the usage meter, the                              
       639 +       media drop zone, the project/workspace browser, the Re
           +motion preview (sandboxed iframe),                           
       640 +       and the EDD inspector/diff viewer.                    
       641 +     - Translate user intent (text, drag-drop, control change
           +s) into Edit/Session Protocol                                
       642 +       requests to the daemon.                               
       643 +     - Stream and render daemon events (agent thinking, tool 
           +progress, render progress, errors)                           
       644 +       over SSE.                                             
       645 +   Explicitly NOT responsible for: filesystem access, process
           + spawning, network egress, secret                            
       646 +   storage. (See Section 23 Security.)                       
       647 +   Deep dive: docs/13-ux-and-terminal.md, docs/04-system-arch
           +itecture.md.                                                 
       648 +                                                             
       649 + 8.3  The Daemon (control plane) - the only privileged proces
           +s                                                            
       650 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       651 +   Stack: a single long-lived Node 24 process. In the simples
           +t topology it is the Electron main                           
       652 +   process; for robustness it MAY be a forked/utility service
           + so a renderer crash never takes                             
       653 +   down in-flight renders. It exposes a local HTTP + SSE inte
           +rface (loopback only, token-guarded)                         
       654 +   for the cockpit, exactly as open-design's daemon does.    
       655 +   Core modules:                                             
       656 +     - Session Manager: owns Claude CLI sessions (create/resu
           +me/interrupt), maps cockpit                                  
       657 +       conversations to CLI session IDs, manages plan/auto mo
           +de and permission prompts.                                   
       658 +     - Tool Manager + OpenVideo MCP server: registers and run
           +s the deterministic media tools as                           
       659 +       MCP tools (Section 8.6); enforces per-tool permissions
           + and sandboxing.                                             
       660 +     - Render Queue + Background Workers: schedules and runs 
           +render jobs (the execution DAG;                              
       661 +       Section 14), reports progress, supports cancellation, 
           +survives renderer restarts.                                  
       662 +     - Installation Agent: hardware detection and tiered depe
           +ndency provisioning (Section 10).                            
       663 +     - Workspace / File Ops: all reads/writes within the proj
           +ect sandbox; path validation.                                
       664 +     - Version Control: git-backs the EDD and key project sta
           +te; every applied edit is a commit.                          
       665 +     - BYOK Proxy: optional outbound proxy for any user-confi
           +gured OpenAI-compatible or provider                          
       666 +       endpoint (for plugins), with SSRF protection (Section 
           +23).                                                         
       667 +     - Cache Manager: content-addressed render/asset cache (S
           +ection 14).                                                  
       668 +     - Telemetry / Diagnostics / Crash Recovery: local logs, 
           +opt-in telemetry, journaled state                            
       669 +       for resume-after-crash (Section 24, 25).              
       670 +   Deep dive: docs/04-system-architecture.md.                
       671 +                                                             
       672 + 8.4  The Reasoning Plane (the Claude CLI)                   
       673 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       674 +   OpenVideo spawns the Claude CLI headless as a child of the
           + daemon (ADR-0002). The daemon                               
       675 +   constructs the prompt and options (model, effort, permissi
           +on mode, MCP config, the project's                           
       676 +   STYLE.md and EDD as context), spawns the CLI in stream-jso
           +n mode, and parses the event stream                          
       677 +   (thinking, tool_use, tool_result, usage, result). The Dire
           +ctor agent and all specialized                               
       678 +   subagents are defined as Claude Code subagents + skills sh
           +ipped inside the OpenVideo project                           
       679 +   scaffold (Section 9). The CLI calls deterministic tools th
           +rough the OpenVideo MCP server.                              
       680 +   Auth: the CLI runs on the user's Claude subscription (no p
           +er-token API key required by                                 
       681 +   default). The Claude Agent SDK is the documented alternati
           +ve for environments that prefer                              
       682 +   an in-process, API-keyed library (ADR-0002).              
       683 +   Deep dive: docs/05-agent-architecture.md, docs/11-prompt-a
           +nd-intent-engine.md, Appendix C.                             
       684 +                                                             
       685 + 8.5  The Video Engine and Compiler                          
       686 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       687 +   The engine turns intent into a render. It comprises: the I
           +ntent/Prompt engine (Section 16),                            
       688 +   the Planner (Section 9), the EDD/Video-AST and its schema 
           +(Section 13), the compiler that                              
       689 +   lowers EDD -> IR -> execution DAG (Section 12), and the re
           +nder scheduler/executor (Section 14)                         
       690 +   that drives the rendering engine (Section 15). It lives in
           + the daemon (so it is privileged and                         
       691 +   deterministic), and is invoked both directly (deterministi
           +c recompiles) and by agents via MCP                          
       692 +   tools (e.g. "apply this EDD patch", "render preview of seg
           +ment").                                                      
       693 +   Deep dive: docs/07-video-engine-and-compiler.md, docs/08-e
           +xecution-and-render-graph.md.                                
       694 +                                                             
       695 + 8.6  The Tool Surface - the OpenVideo MCP server            
       696 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       697 +   All deterministic capability is exposed to agents as MCP t
           +ools through a single stdio MCP                              
       698 +   server run by the daemon. Representative tools (full catal
           +og in docs/05 and Appendix D):                               
       699 +     probe(media)                 -> media metadata (ffprobe)
       700 +     extract_audio(media)         -> wav                     
       701 +     transcribe(audio, opts)      -> transcript + segment/wor
           +d timings (Whisper/faster-whisper)                           
       702 +     detect_silence(audio, opts)  -> silence/hesitation range
           +s                                                            
       703 +     detect_cuts(video, opts)     -> cut timestamps + scores 
       704 +     tonemap_grade(video, look)   -> graded SDR a-roll (zscal
           +e/tonemap + grade)                                           
       705 +     level_audio(audio, target)   -> loudnorm + denoise (two-
           +pass)                                                        
       706 +     edd_apply_patch(patch)       -> mutate the EDD (validate
           +d)                                                           
       707 +     edd_render(range, quality)   -> render preview/final via
           + the compiler+engine                                         
       708 +     remotion_render(comp, props) -> graphics/caption PNG seq
           +uence or MP4                                                 
       709 +     ffmpeg_compose(spec)         -> composite/encode (typed 
           +spec, not raw shell)                                         
       710 +     fetch_media(url)             -> sandboxed import (yt-dlp
           +), permission-gated                                          
       711 +   Tools are typed, validated, permissioned, and sandboxed. A
           +gents never receive a raw shell for                          
       712 +   privileged actions; a constrained bash tool MAY exist for 
           +breadth but high-risk actions are                            
       713 +   promoted to dedicated, gated tools (the agent-design princ
           +iple from the Claude API guidance).                          
       714 +   Deep dive: docs/05-agent-architecture.md, docs/15-plugin-s
           +dk.md.                                                       
       715 +                                                             
       716 + 8.7  Protocols and IPC                                      
       717 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       718 +   - Cockpit <-> Daemon: the "Edit/Session Protocol" - a docu
           +mented request/response + event                              
       719 +     protocol (LSP-inspired). Requests over local HTTP (loopb
           +ack, bearer-token), events over SSE.                         
       720 +     Message families: session.* (start/resume/interrupt), in
           +tent.* (submit), plan.* (propose/                            
       721 +     approve/amend), edd.* (get/patch/diff/history), render.*
           + (request/progress/cancel),                                  
       722 +     install.* (status/approve), control.* (model/effort/mode
           +/permission), usage.* (meter).                               
       723 +   - Daemon <-> Claude CLI: spawn + stdio stream-json (Append
           +ix C documents the event schema and                          
       724 +     the versioned adapter that insulates the codebase from C
           +LI changes).                                                 
       725 +   - Daemon <-> Tools: child processes with typed argument co
           +nstruction, captured stdout/stderr,                          
       726 +     progress parsing, timeouts, and cancellation.           
       727 +   - Daemon <-> Disk: all within the project sandbox; content
           +-addressed cache keys.                                       
       728 +   Deep dive: docs/04-system-architecture.md, Appendix C.    
       729 +                                                             
       730 + 8.8  Process and concurrency model                          
       731 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       732 +   - Electron main (or forked daemon): single privileged even
           +t loop; long jobs offloaded to                               
       733 +     worker threads / child processes so the loop stays respo
           +nsive.                                                       
       734 +   - Render workers: a bounded pool (sized to CPU/GPU) drains
           + the render queue; each job is a                             
       735 +     subgraph of the execution DAG. GPU-bound steps (NVENC/CU
           +DA) and CPU-bound steps are                                  
       736 +     scheduled distinctly (Section 22).                      
       737 +   - Claude CLI: one child process per active session; subage
           +nts are managed by the CLI itself.                           
       738 +   - Backpressure: the queue caps concurrent renders and tran
           +scriptions to avoid thrashing;                               
       739 +     progress and ETA are streamed to the cockpit.           
       740 +                                                             
       741 + 8.9  End-to-end data flow (the canonical sequence)          
       742 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       743 +   1. User drops a clip and types intent in the cockpit.     
       744 +   2. Cockpit -> daemon: intent.submit (with project + contro
           +l settings).                                                 
       745 +   3. Daemon ensures dependencies (Installation Agent) and bu
           +ilds the prompt/options.                                     
       746 +   4. Daemon spawns/*resumes* the Claude CLI session; streams
           + events to the cockpit.                                      
       747 +   5. Director plans (plan mode): produces a creative bluepri
           +nt; cockpit shows it for approval.                           
       748 +   6. On approval, agents call MCP tools to research footage 
           +and assemble/patch the EDD.                                  
       749 +   7. Daemon validates each EDD patch (schema + lint) and com
           +mits it to git.                                              
       750 +   8. Compiler lowers EDD -> IR -> execution DAG; scheduler r
           +enders (incremental, cached).                                
       751 +   9. Preview frames/clips stream to the sandboxed preview; Q
           +A/Critique agent reviews.                                    
       752 +   10. On acceptance, the Export agent produces the final pla
           +tform-optimized file; daemon                                 
       753 +       reports completion; the EDD + render are versioned.   
       754 +

       799 + 8.11  Technology stack (summary)                            
       800 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       801 +   Shell/UI       : Electron, Next.js, React, TypeScript     
       802 +   Daemon         : Node 24, TypeScript, Express (or Fastify)
           + + SSE, better-sqlite3 (project DB),                         
       803 +                    simple-git (or libgit2 binding) for EDD v
           +ersioning                                                    
       804 +   Agent          : Claude CLI (headless, stream-json); model
           +s claude-opus-4-8 / -sonnet-4-6 /                            
       805 +                    -haiku-4-5; MCP (stdio)                  
       806 +   Media tools    : FFmpeg, FFprobe, Whisper / faster-whisper
           + (bundled Python+torch toolchain),                           
       807 +                    Remotion (headless Chrome), yt-dlp, Image
           +Magick                                                       
       808 +   Packaging      : pnpm monorepo; electron-builder; winget/c
           +hoco-assisted installs (Windows)                             
       809 +   Render         : Remotion + FFmpeg; NVENC/CUDA when presen
           +t, CPU fallback always                                       
       810 +   Deep dive: docs/04-system-architecture.md.                
       811 +                                                             
       812 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
       813 + 9. AGENT ARCHITECTURE                                       
       814 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
       815 +                                                             
       816 + 9.1  Philosophy                                             
       817 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       818 + One monolithic prompt cannot reliably direct a multi-stage c
           +reative pipeline. OpenVideo uses a                           
       819 + director-plus-specialists model: a Director orchestrates a r
           +oster of narrow, expert subagents,                           
       820 + each with a single responsibility, its own tools, its own me
           +mory, and a defined failure policy.                          
       821 + This mirrors how Claude Code uses subagents (isolated contex
           +t, parallelism, specialization) and                          
       822 + how a real production team is organized (a creative director
           + coordinating editors, colorists,                            
       823 + sound, motion, and QA).                                     
       824 +                                                             
       825 + Design rules:                                               
       826 +   - Narrow remit per agent. An agent that does one thing can
           + be evaluated, cached, and retried.                          
       827 +   - Isolated context. Subagents get only the context they ne
           +ed (the relevant EDD slice, the                              
       828 +     STYLE.md, their inputs), keeping token cost and confusio
           +n down.                                                      
       829 +   - Cheap where possible. Mechanical subagents (e.g. probing
           +, validation, simple extraction) run                         
       830 +     on claude-haiku-4-5 or are pure deterministic tools; cre
           +ative/judgment agents run on                                 
       831 +     claude-opus-4-8 (or -sonnet-4-6) with higher effort.    
       832 +   - Data in, data out. Agents communicate through the EDD an
           +d typed messages, not free prose.                            
       833 +   - Bounded autonomy. Plan/auto mode and the permission syst
           +em gate hard-to-reverse actions.                             
       834 +                                                             
       835 + 9.2  How agents are realized on the Claude CLI              
       836 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       837 +   - The Director is the top-level CLI session. The daemon se
           +eds it with the system prompt, the                           
       838 +     project STYLE.md, the current EDD, and the available MCP
           + tools.                                                      
       839 +   - Specialized subagents are defined as Claude Code subagen
           +ts (agent definition files) shipped                          
       840 +     in the OpenVideo scaffold (under the project's agents/ a
           +nd the app's bundled skills). The                            
       841 +     Director delegates to them.                             
       842 +   - Skills (SKILL.md) encode task playbooks (e.g. "premium r
           +eel caption styling", "HLG->SDR                              
       843 +     grade recipe") that agents load on demand.              
       844 +   - Tools are the OpenVideo MCP server (Section 8.6). Anthro
           +pic/CLI tools (read/write/bash/etc.)                         
       845 +     are available but high-risk actions are promoted to gate
           +d MCP tools.                                                 
       846 +   - The orchestration loop is plan -> approve -> execute -> 
           +review -> refine (Section 11).                               
       847 +   Deep dive: docs/05-agent-architecture.md, docs/11-prompt-a
           +nd-intent-engine.md.                                         
       848 +                                                             
       849 + 9.3  Agent roster (overview)                                
       850 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       851 +   Tier        Agent                  One-line remit         
           +                Default model                                
       852 +   ----------  ---------------------  -----------------------
           +--------------  ----------------                             
       853 +   Orchestr.   Director               Own the goal; plan; del
           +egate; accept   opus-4-8 (xhigh)                             
       854 +   Planning    Planner                Turn intent+footage int
           +o a blueprint   opus-4-8 (high)                              
       855 +   Planning    Research               Gather facts/refs (web/
           +asset search)   sonnet-4-6                                   
       856 +   Analysis    Transcript             ASR + authoritative tra
           +nscript         haiku/tool + opus                            
       857 +   Analysis    Audio                  Loudness/denoise/EQ pla
           +n + verify      sonnet-4-6                                   
       858 +   Analysis    Color                  Tonemap+grade plan + ve
           +rify            sonnet-4-6                                   
       859 +   Creative    Story/Retention/Hook   Narrative spine, pacing
           +, hook rebuild  opus-4-8 (high)                              
       860 +   Creative    Caption                Word-level captions, ro
           +manization,     opus-4-8 (high)                              
       861 +                                      emphasis               
       862 +   Creative    Motion/Animation       Remotion components (gr
           +aphics)         sonnet-4-6                                   
       863 +   Creative    B-roll                 Copyright-safe b-roll p
           +lan + assets    sonnet-4-6                                   
       864 +   Creative    Music/SFX              Royalty-safe bed + cues
           + + ducking      sonnet-4-6                                   
       865 +   Publishing  Thumbnail/Title/Meta   Cover frame, titles, ca
           +ptions/hashtags sonnet-4-6                                   
       866 +   Quality     QA/Critique            Score output; demand re
           +visions         opus-4-8 (high)                              
       867 +   Quality     Simulation             Predict retention/legib
           +ility issues    sonnet-4-6                                   
       868 +   Quality     Validation             Schema/lint/contract ch
           +ecks            haiku/tool                                   
       869 +   Systems     Optimization/Perf      Compress, proxy, schedu
           +le, cost        sonnet-4-6                                   
       870 +   Systems     Export                 Final platform-optimize
           +d encode        haiku/tool + check                           
       871 +   Systems     Installation           Prepare the machine (Se
           +ction 10)       sonnet-4-6                                   
       872 +                                                             
       873 + 9.4  Per-agent specifications                               
       874 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
       875 + Each agent is specified with the same template: Remit | Inpu
           +ts | Outputs | Memory | Tools |                              
       876 + Permissions | Comms | Failure/Retry | Delegation | Context s
           +trategy | Reasoning/effort. Where a                          
       877 + field is obvious or shared, it is stated briefly. Full prose
           + specs: docs/05-agent-architecture.md.                       
       878 +                                                             
       879 + --- DIRECTOR AGENT ---                                      
       880 +   Remit: Own the user's goal end to end; produce/seek approv
           +al of the plan; delegate to                                  
       881 +     specialists; integrate results; decide when the result m
           +eets the bar; report.                                        
       882 +   Inputs: user intent, project STYLE.md, current EDD, contro
           +l settings (model/effort/mode),                              
       883 +     usage budget.                                           
       884 +   Outputs: an approved plan; a sequence of delegations; a fi
           +nal accepted EDD + render.                                   
       885 +   Memory: the session transcript; the project memory dir; th
           +e plan and its revisions.                                    
       886 +   Tools: all MCP tools (mostly via delegation); plan/approva
           +l tools; EDD read.                                           
       887 +   Permissions: high (can trigger renders and exports - gated
           + by mode/permission prompts).                                
       888 +   Comms: receives intent from daemon; emits delegations and 
           +status; requests user approval in                            
       889 +     plan mode.                                              
       890 +   Failure/Retry: on subagent failure, retry with adjusted in
           +structions or reassign; escalate to                          
       891 +     the user if blocked; never loop unboundedly (effort/turn
           + budget).                                                    
       892 +   Delegation: chooses agents per stage; runs independent age
           +nts in parallel (e.g. Transcript +                           
       893 +     Color + Audio analysis concurrently).                   
       894 +   Context strategy: keeps a compact running state; passes on
           +ly relevant slices to subagents;                             
       895 +     relies on compaction for long sessions.                 
       896 +   Reasoning/effort: opus-4-8 at xhigh for planning/integrati
           +on; lower for routine coordination.                          
       897 +                                                             
       898 + --- PLANNER AGENT ---                                       
       899 +   Remit: Convert intent + footage analysis into an explicit 
           +creative blueprint (the structured                           
       900 +     precursor to the EDD): narrative spine, section-by-secti
           +on timeline, hook plan, b-roll list,                         
       901 +     motion-graphics list, caption style, audio plan, color p
           +lan, export target.                                          
       902 +   Inputs: intent, transcript, cut list, silence map, probe m
           +etadata, STYLE.md, look references.                          
       903 +   Outputs: a blueprint document + an initial EDD skeleton (v
           +alidated).                                                   
       904 +   Memory: plan history (versioned).                         
       905 +   Tools: probe, transcribe (read), detect_cuts/silence (read
           +), edd_apply_patch (skeleton).                               
       906 +   Permissions: medium (no render/export).                   
       907 +   Failure/Retry: if inputs missing, request the relevant ana
           +lysis agent first; re-plan on                                
       908 +     critique feedback.                                      
       909 +   Delegation: requests analysis agents; hands the blueprint 
           +to creative agents.                                          
       910 +   Context strategy: loads only the transcript + metadata sum
           +maries, not raw media.                                       
       911 +   Reasoning/effort: opus-4-8 high.                          
       912 +                                                             
       913 + --- RESEARCH AGENT ---                                      
       914 +   Remit: Gather external facts/refs when needed (e.g. verify
           + a claim, find a style reference,                            
       915 +     locate a royalty-free asset source) - copyright- and pol
           +icy-safe only.                                               
       916 +   Inputs: a research question + constraints.                
       917 +   Outputs: cited findings / candidate asset references (neve
           +r scraped copyrighted media).                                
       918 +   Tools: web search/fetch (via CLI server tools or a permiss
           +ioned proxy); asset-search plugins.                          
       919 +   Permissions: network (gated; SSRF-guarded proxy).         
       920 +   Failure/Retry: degrade to "unable to verify"; never fabric
           +ate.                                                         
       921 +   Reasoning/effort: sonnet-4-6.                             
       922 +                                                             
       923 + --- TRANSCRIPT AGENT ---                                    
       924 +   Remit: Produce the authoritative transcript with reliable 
           +timings; handle code-switching;                              
       925 +     decide model size/device with the user (tiered).        
       926 +   Inputs: audio, language hints, device/model policy.       
       927 +   Outputs: transcript (text) + segment timings + word timing
           +s (or distributed words); the                                
       928 +     authoritative text that overrides ASR errors.           
       929 +   Memory: per-project transcript (versioned).               
       930 +   Tools: extract_audio, transcribe (Whisper/faster-whisper),
           + align (optional WhisperX).                                  
       931 +   Permissions: local compute (may request GPU enablement via
           + Installation Agent).                                        
       932 +   Failure/Retry: if small model is poor (PoC F4), escalate t
           +o a capable model; if CPU is too                             
       933 +     slow, offer GPU setup.                                  
       934 +   Reasoning/effort: mostly tool-driven; opus-4-8 only for co
           +rrection/romanization handoff.                               
       935 +                                                             
       936 + --- AUDIO AGENT ---                                         
       937 +   Remit: Plan and verify the voice chain (HPF/denoise/de-ess
           +/EQ/compress), loudness target,                              
       938 +     limiter; plan music ducking and SFX placement; verify me
           +asured loudness.                                             
       939 +   Inputs: audio, target standard (default -14 LUFS), measure
           +d stats.                                                     
       940 +   Outputs: an audio-processing spec in the EDD + verificatio
           +n (measured I/TP).                                           
       941 +   Tools: level_audio (two-pass loudnorm + afftdn), probe, ff
           +mpeg_compose (audio).                                        
       942 +   Permissions: medium.                                      
       943 +   Failure/Retry: re-measure and re-apply if target missed; f
           +lag if source is unrecoverable.                              
       944 +   Reasoning/effort: sonnet-4-6.                             
       945 +                                                             
       946 + --- COLOR AGENT ---                                         
       947 +   Remit: Detect HDR/HLG vs SDR; plan tonemap + a tasteful gr
           +ade (white balance, contrast, skin                           
       948 +     protection, vibrance, light sharpen); avoid over-grading
           +; verify with before/after frames.                           
       949 +   Inputs: video, look/STYLE.md, probe color metadata.       
       950 +   Outputs: a color spec in the EDD + sample frames.         
       951 +   Tools: tonemap_grade (zscale/tonemap chain), probe, edd_re
           +nder (sample frames).                                        
       952 +   Permissions: medium.                                      
       953 +   Failure/Retry: fall back to conservative grade if the look
           + is ambiguous.                                               
       954 +   Reasoning/effort: sonnet-4-6.                             
       955 +                                                             
       956 + --- STORY / RETENTION / HOOK AGENT ---                      
       957 +   Remit: Define the narrative spine (promise->authority->ten
           +sion->resolution->CTA); maximize                             
       958 +     retention; rebuild the first 3 seconds; mark dead air, h
           +esitations, repetition for cutting;                          
       959 +     enforce "no static frame > 3-4s".                       
       960 +   Inputs: transcript, cut list, silence map, intent, STYLE.m
           +d.                                                           
       961 +   Outputs: pacing + smart-cut decisions + hook plan, encoded
           + as EDD patches.                                             
       962 +   Tools: detect_silence/cuts (read), edd_apply_patch.       
       963 +   Permissions: medium.                                      
       964 +   Failure/Retry: respect "preserve natural speech"; if over-
           +cutting risk, prefer fewer cuts.                             
       965 +   Reasoning/effort: opus-4-8 high.                          
       966 +                                                             
       967 + --- CAPTION AGENT ---                                       
       968 +   Remit: Produce word-level captions with karaoke timing, em
           +phasis on key terms, and correct                             
       969 +     romanization for code-switched speech (e.g. natural Hing
           +lish, not mechanical transliteration                         
       970 +     - PoC F5); keep captions off the eyeline; sync <= 80 ms.
       971 +   Inputs: authoritative transcript + word/segment timings, S
           +TYLE.md caption style.                                       
       972 +   Outputs: a captions structure in the EDD (words, timings, 
           +emphasis, style) consumed by the                             
       973 +     Motion agent / Remotion caption component.              
       974 +   Tools: transcribe (read), edd_apply_patch; Caption-style p
           +lugins.                                                      
       975 +   Permissions: medium.                                      
       976 +   Failure/Retry: if timings are coarse, distribute words wit
           +hin segment; spot-check sync.                                
       977 +   Reasoning/effort: opus-4-8 high (romanization + emphasis a
           +re judgment tasks).                                          
       978 +                                                             
       979 + --- MOTION / ANIMATION AGENT ---                            
       980 +   Remit: Author the Remotion components for graphics, overla
           +ys, captions, lower-thirds, kinetic                          
       981 +     headlines, comparison cards, flow diagrams, timelines, C
           +TA - on brand, deterministic.                                
       982 +   Inputs: EDD graphics/caption specs, STYLE.md tokens, brand
           + assets.                                                     
       983 +   Outputs: Remotion component props/compositions referenced 
           +by the EDD; preview frames.                                  
       984 +   Tools: remotion_render, edd_apply_patch; animation-pack pl
           +ugins.                                                       
       985 +   Permissions: medium.                                      
       986 +   Failure/Retry: if the native compositor fails, the render 
           +engine falls back to PNG-sequence +                          
       987 +     FFmpeg automatically (ADR-0006); the agent need not hand
           +le it.                                                       
       988 +   Reasoning/effort: sonnet-4-6.                             
       989 +                                                             
       990 + --- B-ROLL AGENT ---                                        
       991 +   Remit: Propose and place copyright-safe b-roll that reinfo
           +rces the spoken content (timing,                             
       992 +     duration, transition, opacity, blend, motion); prefer ge
           +nerated vector/graphics or licensed                          
       993 +     stills; never scrape copyrighted footage.               
       994 +   Inputs: transcript, narrative spine, STYLE.md.            
       995 +   Outputs: b-roll entries in the EDD + generated/sourced ass
           +ets.                                                         
       996 +   Tools: remotion_render (vector b-roll), fetch_media (only 
           +authorized/royalty-free), gen-image                          
       997 +     plugins (optional, licensed).                           
       998 +   Permissions: network (gated) for authorized sources only. 
       999 +   Failure/Retry: if no safe asset, fall back to on-brand vec
           +tor graphics.                                                
      1000 +   Reasoning/effort: sonnet-4-6.                             
      1001 +                                                             
      1002 + --- MUSIC / SFX AGENT ---                                   
      1003 +   Remit: Add a royalty-safe music bed (ducked under voice) a
           +nd SFX cues (impacts, whooshes,                              
      1004 +     pops, stamps, chimes) on beats; never use copyrighted au
           +dio.                                                         
      1005 +   Inputs: EDD beats, intent, user-supplied or royalty-free l
           +ibraries.                                                    
      1006 +   Outputs: music/SFX entries + mix spec (sidechain ducking) 
           +in the EDD.                                                  
      1007 +   Tools: ffmpeg_compose (mix/duck), asset/music-provider plu
           +gins.                                                        
      1008 +   Permissions: medium; network only for authorized providers
           +.                                                            
      1009 +   Failure/Retry: if no licensed track, ship voice-forward an
           +d flag (PoC behavior).                                       
      1010 +   Reasoning/effort: sonnet-4-6.                             
      1011 +                                                             
      1012 + --- THUMBNAIL / TITLE / METADATA AGENT ---                  
      1013 +   Remit: Produce a cover frame/thumbnail, titles, on-screen 
           +title cards, and platform metadata                           
      1014 +     (caption text, hashtags, description) consistent with th
           +e content and STYLE.md.                                      
      1015 +   Inputs: final EDD/render, transcript, intent, platform tar
           +get.                                                         
      1016 +   Outputs: thumbnail asset; title/metadata structures.      
      1017 +   Tools: remotion_render, edd_render (frame grab), edd_apply
           +_patch.                                                      
      1018 +   Permissions: medium.                                      
      1019 +   Reasoning/effort: sonnet-4-6.                             
      1020 +                                                             
      1021 + --- QA / CRITIQUE AGENT ---                                 
      1022 +   Remit: Independently score the output against the brief an
           +d a rubric (hook strength, pacing,                           
      1023 +     caption sync/legibility, grade realism, loudness, brand 
           +fidelity, platform compliance);                              
      1024 +     demand specific revisions; gate acceptance.             
      1025 +   Inputs: rendered preview + frames, the EDD, the brief/rubr
           +ic.                                                          
      1026 +   Outputs: a scored critique with concrete, actionable revis
           +ion requests (or "accept").                                  
      1027 +   Tools: edd_render (frames/clips), probe (loudness/format),
           + vision (frame inspection).                                  
      1028 +   Permissions: read + render.                               
      1029 +   Failure/Retry: iterate with the responsible creative agent
           + until the bar is met or budget                              
      1030 +     is exhausted (then escalate to the user). Report-everyth
           +ing-then-filter discipline.                                  
      1031 +   Reasoning/effort: opus-4-8 high (independent context from 
           +the creators - cross-checking).                              
      1032 +                                                             
      1033 + --- SIMULATION AGENT ---                                    
      1034 +   Remit: Predict likely audience problems before render (e.g
           +. a static stretch, a buried hook,                           
      1035 +     an unreadable caption on small screens, an off-brand col
           +or) and feed them forward.                                   
      1036 +   Inputs: the EDD + sampled frames.                         
      1037 +   Outputs: a risk list with suggested fixes.                
      1038 +   Tools: edd_render (samples), vision.                      
      1039 +   Reasoning/effort: sonnet-4-6.                             
      1040 +                                                             
      1041 + --- VALIDATION AGENT ---                                    
      1042 +   Remit: Enforce contracts: EDD schema validity, asset refer
           +ences resolve, timings monotonic,                            
      1043 +     no edge-clipping, export spec sane. Mostly deterministic
           + (the compiler's validation pass),                           
      1044 +     with an agent wrapper for explanation.                  
      1045 +   Inputs: EDD, asset manifest.                              
      1046 +   Outputs: pass/fail + precise diagnostics.                 
      1047 +   Tools: edd validate (deterministic), probe.               
      1048 +   Reasoning/effort: haiku-4-5 / pure tool.                  
      1049 +                                                             
      1050 + --- OPTIMIZATION / PERFORMANCE AGENT ---                    
      1051 +   Remit: Manage cost and speed: choose proxy vs full, pick G
           +PU vs CPU paths, compress final to                           
      1052 +     platform norms, decide what to cache, and keep within th
           +e usage budget.                                              
      1053 +   Inputs: hardware profile, render graph, usage budget, plat
           +form target.                                                 
      1054 +   Outputs: scheduling/quality decisions; compression setting
           +s.                                                           
      1055 +   Tools: scheduler hints, ffmpeg_compose (compress), cache c
           +ontrols.                                                     
      1056 +   Reasoning/effort: sonnet-4-6.                             
      1057 +                                                             
      1058 + --- EXPORT AGENT ---                                        
      1059 +   Remit: Produce the final platform-optimized deliverable (e
           +.g. H.264 High, AAC 48k, +faststart,                         
      1060 +     1080x1920, 60fps for IG reels), verify it (ffprobe + lou
           +dness), and version it.                                      
      1061 +   Inputs: accepted EDD, platform target.                    
      1062 +   Outputs: final file + verification report.                
      1063 +   Tools: edd_render (final), ffmpeg_compose, probe.         
      1064 +   Reasoning/effort: mostly tool; haiku-4-5 for the verificat
           +ion summary.                                                 
      1065 +                                                             
      1066 + --- INSTALLATION AGENT ---                                  
      1067 +   Remit: Prepare the machine (Section 10). Tiered: core auto
           +; heavy on-demand. Detect hardware;                          
      1068 +     install, verify, repair, roll back; report progress.    
      1069 +   Inputs: hardware profile, the capability a workflow needs.
      1070 +   Outputs: a ready toolchain + a capability report.         
      1071 +   Tools: installer tools (winget/choco/pip/npm wrappers), HW
           + detection, PATH repair.                                     
      1072 +   Permissions: elevated (the one place the product installs 
           +software) - explicit, audited.                               
      1073 +   Reasoning/effort: sonnet-4-6.                             
      1074 +                                                             
      1075 + 9.5  Inter-agent communication protocol                     
      1076 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1077 +   - The shared substrate is the EDD (validated patches) plus
           + typed control messages routed by the                        
      1078 +     Director. Agents do not free-text at each other; they em
           +it structured deltas and findings.                           
      1079 +   - The Director maintains the canonical task state; subagen
           +ts return results to the Director,                           
      1080 +     which integrates and decides next steps (a hub-and-spoke
           + model, with parallel fan-out for                            
      1081 +     independent analysis agents).                           
      1082 +   - All cross-agent artifacts (transcript, plan, EDD, critiq
           +ue) are written to the project                               
      1083 +     workspace so they are inspectable and versioned.        
      1084 +                                                             
      1085 + 9.6  Shared memory model                                    
      1086 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1087 +   - Session memory: the CLI session transcript (compacted as
           + needed).                                                    
      1088 +   - Project memory: a memory/ directory (per-project facts, 
           +style decisions, prior critiques) the                        
      1089 +     agents can read/write, surviving sessions.              
      1090 +   - Artifact memory: the versioned EDD, transcript, plan, an
           +d renders (git history) are the                              
      1091 +     durable record of every decision.                       
      1092 +                                                             
      1093 + 9.7  Failure handling, retries, escalation                  
      1094 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1095 +   - Deterministic tool failure: captured (stderr, exit code)
           +, classified, and either auto-retried                        
      1096 +     (transient), routed to a fallback (e.g. compositor -> PN
           +G-sequence), or surfaced to the agent                        
      1097 +     with a precise diagnostic.                              
      1098 +   - Agent failure / low-quality output: the QA/Critique loop
           + demands revision; bounded by an                             
      1099 +     effort/turn budget; on exhaustion, escalate to the user 
           +with the best result + the open issue.                       
      1100 +   - Hard blockers (missing capability): the Director invokes
           + the Installation Agent or asks the                          
      1101 +     user. Never loops unboundedly.                          
      1102 +                                                             
      1103 + 9.8  Context-window management                              
      1104 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1105 +   - Subagents receive only the relevant EDD slice, the STYLE
           +.md, and their inputs - not the whole                        
      1106 +     project. Large artifacts (raw transcripts, frame dumps) 
           +are referenced by path/summary.                              
      1107 +   - Long sessions rely on compaction; stable context (system
           + prompt, STYLE.md, tool list) is                             
      1108 +     ordered first for prompt caching (Section 22).          
      1109 +                                                             
      1110 + 9.9  Reasoning and effort strategy                          
      1111 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1112 +   - Creative/judgment agents (Director, Planner, Story/Reten
           +tion, Caption, QA): opus-4-8 at                              
      1113 +     high/xhigh, adaptive thinking.                          
      1114 +   - Production agents (Audio, Color, Motion, B-roll, Music, 
           +Thumbnail, Optimization, Research,                           
      1115 +     Simulation, Installation): sonnet-4-6.                  
      1116 +   - Mechanical agents (Validation, Export verification, Tran
           +script orchestration): haiku-4-5 or                          
      1117 +     pure tools.                                             
      1118 +   - The user's control surface can globally bias model/effor
           +t (e.g. "fast" vs "max quality").                            
      1119 +   Deep dive: docs/05-agent-architecture.md.                 
      1120 +                                                             
      1121  -------------------------------------------------------------
            -----------------------------------

           -re]                                                          
      1122 + [END OF PART 2 - continues with Section 10: Installation Arc
           +hitecture]

      1118     - The user's control surface can globally bias model/effor
