      1120  
      1121 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1122 + 10. INSTALLATION ARCHITECTURE (THE INSTALLATION AGENT)      
      1123 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1124 +                                                             
      1125 + 10.1  Purpose and model                                     
      1126 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1127 + The Installation Agent gives a fresh machine its "superpower
           +s" before any editing begins. It is                          
      1128 + the single component permitted to install software, and it d
           +oes so on a TIERED basis (ADR-0004):                         
      1129 +                                                             
      1130 +   - CORE tier (auto, silent, fast on first run): the small, 
           +universally-needed toolchain that                            
      1131 +     every workflow depends on - ffmpeg, ffprobe, yt-dlp, Nod
           +e/pnpm (if not bundled), and the                             
      1132 +     Remotion runtime. These are quick to install and small. 
      1133 +   - HEAVY tier (on first use, one-tap confirm): large or har
           +dware-specific items that not every                          
      1134 +     user needs immediately - Whisper / faster-whisper plus a
           + bundled Python+torch toolchain and                          
      1135 +     model weights (~1.5 GB+), CUDA/cuDNN builds for NVIDIA G
           +PUs, optional model packs, large                             
      1136 +     fonts/codecs. The agent explains the download size and r
           +eason, then proceeds on approval.                            
      1137 +                                                             
      1138 + This directly answers the proof-of-concept's biggest frictio
           +n (F2, F3): no manual installs, no                           
      1139 + multi-gigabyte surprises, and a known-good toolchain rather 
           +than a fragile system Python.                                
      1140 +                                                             
      1141 + 10.2  Hardware and OS detection                             
      1142 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1143 + On first run (and on demand), the agent profiles the machine
           +:                                                            
      1144 +   - OS + version + architecture (Windows 10/11 x64 first; ma
           +cOS arm64/x64 and Linux later).                              
      1145 +   - CPU (cores, features), RAM, free disk on the target volu
           +me.                                                          
      1146 +   - GPU: vendor/model and capability (NVIDIA + CUDA version 
           ++ driver; later AMD/Intel; Apple                             
      1147 +     Metal on macOS). The PoC machine (RTX 3050, CUDA present
           +) is the canonical Windows target.                           
      1148 +   - Existing tools on PATH and their versions (ffmpeg, node,
           + python, git, etc.).                                         
      1149 +   - Available package managers (winget, choco on Windows).  
      1150 + The profile is cached and drives every install decision (e.g
           +. CUDA build only if a supported                             
      1151 + NVIDIA GPU + driver is present; CPU torch otherwise).       
      1152 +                                                             
      1153 + 10.3  Dependency catalog                                    
      1154 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1155 +   Tier   Dependency            Windows install            Pu
           +rpose                                                        
      1156 +   -----  --------------------  -------------------------   -
           +-------------------------------------                        
      1157 +   core   FFmpeg + FFprobe      winget (Gyan build)         t
           +he render/inspection workhorse                               
      1158 +   core   yt-dlp                winget                      a
           +uthorized media import                                       
      1159 +   core   Node + pnpm           bundled / winget            R
           +emotion + tooling runtime                                    
      1160 +   core   Remotion runtime      pnpm (project-local)        g
           +raphics/captions engine                                      
      1161 +   heavy  Python (pinned)       bundled toolchain           h
           +ost for Whisper/torch (avoid system                          
      1162 +                                                            P
           +ython pitfalls; PoC F3)                                      
      1163 +   heavy  Whisper/faster-whisper pip (pinned)               A
           +SR + timestamps                                              
      1164 +   heavy  torch (CPU or CUDA)   pip (device-aware)          A
           +SR compute; CUDA build iff supported                         
      1165 +   heavy  Whisper model weights download (cached)           A
           +SR models (size-tiered)                                      
      1166 +   heavy  ImageMagick           winget (optional)           i
           +mage ops for some plugins                                    
      1167 +   heavy  CUDA/cuDNN runtime    vendor/bundled (if NVIDIA)  G
           +PU acceleration for ASR/encode                               
      1168 +   opt    Fonts / codec packs   bundled/winget              c
           +aption typefaces; extra codecs                               
      1169 +                                                             
      1170 + The catalog is data-driven (a manifest), so plugins can decl
           +are additional dependencies the                              
      1171 + agent provisions on the same tiered, verified basis.        
      1172 +                                                             
      1173 + 10.4  Install lifecycle (per dependency)                    
      1174 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1175 +   detect  -> is it present and the right version? (probe PAT
           +H + version string)                                          
      1176 +   plan    -> choose method (winget/choco/pip/pnpm/bundled) a
           +nd exact pinned version for the                              
      1177 +              detected OS/arch/GPU; compute download size; (h
           +eavy) request confirm                                        
      1178 +   install -> run the installer with captured output and a ti
           +meout; stream progress                                       
      1179 +   configure -> fix PATH (user scope), set env (e.g. PYTHONUT
           +F8=1 to avoid Windows cp1252 console                         
      1180 +              errors - PoC), wire project-local paths        
      1181 +   verify  -> run a known-good smoke test (e.g. `ffmpeg -vers
           +ion`, a 1-frame transcode, a tiny                            
      1182 +              transcription); confirm the capability actually
           + works, not just that a binary exists                        
      1183 +   repair  -> on a broken/partial install (e.g. a corrupted b
           +inary, a merged/duplicated runtime -                         
      1184 +              the PoC saw a doubled ffmpeg in the Remotion co
           +mpositor), reinstall cleanly                                 
      1185 +   rollback -> on failure, restore the prior state (uninstall
           + the partial, revert PATH/env) so the                        
      1186 +              machine is never left half-broken              
      1187 +   report  -> a capability report to the cockpit (what's read
           +y, what's pending, sizes, versions)                          
      1188 +                                                             
      1189 + Idempotency is mandatory: re-running install is safe and a n
           +o-op when everything is healthy.                             
      1190 +                                                             
      1191 + 10.5  Windows-first specifics                               
      1192 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1193 +   - Prefer winget; fall back to choco; bundle where a manage
           +r is unreliable.                                             
      1194 +   - PATH edits are user-scoped and applied so new terminals/
           +sessions see them; the daemon also                           
      1195 +     resolves tool paths directly (not relying solely on inhe
           +rited PATH).                                                 
      1196 +   - Set PYTHONUTF8=1 to avoid the legacy cp1252 console cras
           +h on multilingual output (PoC).                              
      1197 +   - Bundle a pinned Python + torch rather than relying on th
           +e system Python (the PoC's Python                            
      1198 +     3.14 lacked CUDA torch wheels; a bundled, known-good too
           +lchain removes that class of failure).                       
      1199 +   - Detect and avoid the Remotion native-compositor failure 
           +mode by health-checking it and                               
      1200 +     defaulting to the PNG-sequence + FFmpeg render path when
           + it is unhealthy (ADR-0006, Section 15).                     
      1201 +                                                             
      1202 + 10.6  GPU / CUDA strategy                                   
      1203 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1204 +   - If a supported NVIDIA GPU + driver is detected, the heav
           +y tier installs the CUDA torch build                         
      1205 +     and (if needed) CUDA/cuDNN runtime, enabling 30-50x fast
           +er ASR and NVENC-accelerated encode.                         
      1206 +   - Otherwise CPU torch + libx264 are used (always-works fal
           +lback), with the agent clearly noting                        
      1207 +     the speed trade-off and offering GPU enablement when har
           +dware allows.                                                
      1208 +   - The choice is explicit and user-aware (PoC lesson): neve
           +r silently saddle the user with a                            
      1209 +     40-minute CPU transcription when a one-time GPU setup wo
           +uld make it a minute.                                        
      1210 +                                                             
      1211 + 10.7  Progress reporting and UX                             
      1212 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1213 +   - Every step streams structured progress to the cockpit (p
           +hase, percent, ETA, current action),                         
      1214 +     rendered in the "alive" terminal and an install panel.  
      1215 +   - Heavy-tier downloads show size and reason and require on
           +e tap to proceed.                                            
      1216 +   - Failures surface a precise, actionable diagnostic and th
           +e rollback result.                                           
      1217 +   - A "doctor" command re-profiles and self-heals (Section 2
           +5).                                                          
      1218 +                                                             
      1219 + 10.8  Upgrades and pinning                                  
      1220 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1221 +   - All versions are pinned per release for reproducibility;
           + upgrades are deliberate and verified.                       
      1222 +   - The agent can detect outdated tools and offer upgrades w
           +ith rollback safety.                                         
      1223 +   Deep dive: docs/06-installation-agent.md.                 
      1224 +                                                             
      1225 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1226 + 11. VIDEO PIPELINE (INTENT TO RENDER, END TO END)           
      1227 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1228 +                                                             
      1229 + 11.1  The canonical pipeline                                
      1230 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1231 + Every video workflow flows through the same stages. Stages a
           +re agent- or tool-driven, and each                           
      1232 + produces inspectable, versioned artifacts.                  
      1233 +                                                             
      1234 +   (0) ENSURE       capabilities present (Installation Agent;
           + tiered)                                                     
      1235 +   (1) INGEST       import/probe media; create/locate the pro
           +ject; register assets (hashed)                               
      1236 +   (2) ANALYZE      transcript (ASR), cut detection, silence/
           +hesitation, loudness stats, color                            
      1237 +                    metadata, scene/energy analysis  [agents:
           + Transcript, Audio, Color; tools]                            
      1238 +   (3) PLAN         creative blueprint: spine, hook, pacing, 
           +captions, b-roll, graphics, audio,                           
      1239 +                    color, export target  [agent: Planner/Dir
           +ector; plan mode -> user approval]                           
      1240 +   (4) ASSEMBLE     build/patch the EDD (Video AST) from the 
           +blueprint  [creative agents]                                 
      1241 +   (5) COMPILE      EDD -> IR -> execution DAG (validate, lin
           +t, optimize, schedule)  [compiler]                           
      1242 +   (6) RENDER       execute the DAG: smart-cut, grade, audio 
           +mix, Remotion graphics/captions,                             
      1243 +                    FFmpeg composite; preview-quality first, 
           +final later  [scheduler + engine]                            
      1244 +   (7) REVIEW       QA/Critique + Simulation score the result
           +; request revisions (loop to 4-6)                            
      1245 +   (8) EXPORT       final platform-optimized encode + verific
           +ation (ffprobe + loudness)  [Export]                         
      1246 +   (9) VERSION      commit the EDD + render; record provenanc
           +e  [daemon/git]                                              
      1247 +                                                             
      1248 + 11.2  Stage detail                                          
      1249 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1250 +   INGEST: probe() yields duration, resolution, fps, codecs, 
           +color metadata (e.g. HLG/HDR),                               
      1251 +     audio layout. Assets are copied/linked into the project 
           +and content-hashed for caching.                              
      1252 +   ANALYZE: runs analysis agents in parallel where independen
           +t (Transcript || Color || Audio).                            
      1253 +     Produces transcript+timings, cut list, silence map, loud
           +ness stats, color profile.                                   
      1254 +   PLAN: the Planner composes the blueprint; in plan mode the
           + cockpit shows it for approval/edit                          
      1255 +     (the user can say "make the hook punchier", "fewer graph
           +ics", "keep it under 30s").                                  
      1256 +   ASSEMBLE: creative agents translate the approved blueprint
           + into EDD patches (tracks, clips,                            
      1257 +     transitions, effects, captions, graphics, audio, color, 
           +export spec). Each patch is validated                        
      1258 +     and committed.                                          
      1259 +   COMPILE + RENDER + REVIEW + EXPORT: Sections 12, 14, 15, 9
           + (QA), 9 (Export).                                           
      1260 +                                                             
      1261 + 11.3  The proven reel pipeline mapped to stages (worked exam
           +ple)                                                         
      1262 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1263 +   Intent: "Turn this into a premium Instagram Reel."        
      1264 +     INGEST   : probe iPhone 1080x1920 60fps HLG clip.       
      1265 +     ANALYZE  : transcribe (Hindi/English); detect ~20 cuts; 
           +silence map (lead-in trim);                                  
      1266 +                measure loudness (-21 LUFS); detect HLG color
           +.                                                            
      1267 +     PLAN     : spine = promise->authority->tension->resoluti
           +on->CTA; hook rebuild; word-level                            
      1268 +                Hinglish captions w/ emphasis; b-roll/graphic
           +s list; audio to -14 LUFS; HLG->SDR                          
      1269 +                grade; export 1080x1920 H.264/AAC.  [shown fo
           +r approval]                                                  
      1270 +     ASSEMBLE : EDD with a-roll (graded), alternating breathe
           + punch-ins on cuts, caption track,                           
      1271 +                graphics sequences (hook, checklist, VOID/VOI
           +DABLE, flow, timeline, CTA), audio                           
      1272 +                mix, export spec.                            
      1273 +     COMPILE  : validate timings/refs; optimize (proxy for pr
           +eview); schedule.                                            
      1274 +     RENDER   : smart-cut + grade (FFmpeg); captions/graphics
           + (Remotion -> PNG seq if compositor                          
      1275 +                unhealthy); composite + mux (FFmpeg).        
      1276 +     REVIEW   : QA checks hook in <1.5s, caption sync <=80ms,
           + loudness ~-14 LUFS, legibility.                             
      1277 +     EXPORT   : H.264 High, AAC 48k, +faststart, 1080x1920 60
           +fps; verify; version.                                        
      1278 +   This is exactly the PoC's flow, now reproducible and conve
           +rsational.                                                   
      1279 +                                                             
      1280 + 11.4  Preview vs final                                      
      1281 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1282 +   - Preview: low-cost, fast (proxy resolution, draft encode,
           + fewer frames) for the cockpit's                             
      1283 +     sandboxed preview and the QA loop.                      
      1284 +   - Final: full-quality, platform-optimized, verified. Drive
           +n by the same EDD; only quality                              
      1285 +     parameters differ. (Section 15.)                        
      1286 +                                                             
      1287 + 11.5  Determinism and reproducibility                       
      1288 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1289 +   Given the same EDD + assets + tool versions, the render is
           + reproducible (encoder                                       
      1290 +   non-determinism pinned where feasible). The EDD + tool ver
           +sions are recorded with each render,                         
      1291 +   so any output can be regenerated or audited.              
      1292 +   Deep dive: docs/07-video-engine-and-compiler.md, docs/09-r
           +endering-engine.md.                                          
      1293 +                                                             
      1294 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1295 + 12. COMPILER DESIGN (INTENT -> PLAN -> EDD -> IR -> EXECUTIO
           +N DAG)                                                       
      1296 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1297 +                                                             
      1298 + 12.1  Editing as compilation                                
      1299 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1300 + OpenVideo treats an edit as a program to be compiled. This i
           +s the conceptual heart of the system                         
      1301 + and the reason edits are explainable, reproducible, incremen
           +tal, and cacheable. The stages mirror                        
      1302 + a classic compiler (and the tree-sitter / AST / IR / codegen
           + lineage from Section 6.5):                                  
      1303 +                                                             
      1304 +   Front end:  natural-language intent -> (Intent Engine) -> 
           +structured intent                                            
      1305 +               structured intent + footage analysis -> (Plann
           +er) -> creative blueprint                                    
      1306 +   Middle:     blueprint -> (assembly) -> EDD (Video AST)  [t
           +he AST]                                                      
      1307 +               EDD -> (lowering) -> IR  [typed, normalized, r
           +esolution-independent]                                       
      1308 +               IR -> (passes) -> validated, optimized, schedu
           +led IR                                                       
      1309 +   Back end:   IR -> (codegen) -> execution DAG of concrete t
           +ool invocations                                              
      1310 +               DAG -> (scheduler/executor) -> rendered media 
           + [Section 14, 15]                                            
      1311 +                                                             
      1312 + 12.2  Front end - intent and planning                       
      1313 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1314 +   - The Intent Engine (Section 16) classifies the user's req
           +uest into an intent type + parameters                        
      1315 +     (e.g. {goal: make_reel, platform: instagram, style_ref: 
           +hormozi, constraints: {<=30s}}),                             
      1316 +     resolving pronouns/context against the current project a
           +nd EDD.                                                      
      1317 +   - The Planner consumes structured intent + analysis artifa
           +cts and emits a creative blueprint -                         
      1318 +     a human-readable, approvable plan that is also structure
           +d enough to drive assembly.                                  
      1319 +                                                             
      1320 + 12.3  The EDD (Video AST)                                   
      1321 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1322 + The Edit Decision Document is the AST: a typed, JSON, versio
           +n-controlled tree describing the edit                        
      1323 + declaratively and at a high level (intent-bearing), independ
           +ent of concrete tool commands.                               
      1324 +   Top-level shape (schema in Section 13, Appendix D):       
      1325 +     project meta (id, dimensions, fps, color space, platform
           + target, STYLE ref)                                          
      1326 +     sources[]      (assets with hashes, probe metadata)     
      1327 +     timeline       (tracks[]: video/a-roll, b-roll, captions
           +, graphics, audio, music, sfx)                               
      1328 +       clip[]       (source ref, in/out, transforms: crop/sca
           +le/position/speed, punch-in curve)                           
      1329 +       transition[] (type, duration, easing)                 
      1330 +       effect[]     (color grade spec, denoise, sharpen, vign
           +ette - parameterized)                                        
      1331 +     captions       (words[], timings, emphasis, style ref)  
      1332 +     graphics[]     (Remotion component refs + props + time r
           +anges)                                                       
      1333 +     audio          (voice chain, loudness target, music bed 
           ++ ducking, sfx cues)                                         
      1334 +     export         (codec, container, resolution, fps, bitra
           +te, faststart, platform preset)                              
      1335 +     provenance     (which agent authored which node, with ra
           +tionale)                                                     
      1336 +   The EDD is the contract between reasoning (agents author i
           +t) and execution (the compiler                               
      1337 +   consumes it). It is diffable; an "edit" is a validated pat
           +ch + a git commit.                                           
      1338 +                                                             
      1339 + 12.4  Lowering to IR                                        
      1340 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1341 +   The EDD is intent-level and partly abstract (e.g. "alterna
           +ting 3% breathe punch-ins on cuts",                          
      1342 +   "captions in the brand style"). Lowering normalizes it int
           +o a concrete, typed IR:                                      
      1343 +     - resolve style refs/tokens to concrete values (fonts, c
           +olors, sizes from STYLE.md);                                 
      1344 +     - expand high-level directives into explicit per-clip tr
           +ansforms and keyframes (e.g. compute                         
      1345 +       the zoom curve per segment);                          
      1346 +     - resolve asset paths + proxies; normalize time bases to
           + the project fps;                                            
      1347 +     - flatten transitions/effects into ordered, parameterize
           +d operations.                                                
      1348 +   The IR is resolution-independent where possible (so previe
           +w and final share it) and is the unit                        
      1349 +   that the passes operate on.                               
      1350 +                                                             
      1351 + 12.5  Compiler passes                                       
      1352 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1353 +   - Validation pass: schema validity, monotonic timings, res
           +olvable asset refs, in/out within                            
      1354 +     bounds, no caption edge-clipping, sane export spec. Emit
           +s precise diagnostics (Validation                            
      1355 +     agent wraps this for explanation). A failed validation b
           +locks render.                                                
      1356 +   - Lint pass: best-practice warnings (e.g. "static frame > 
           +3-4s", "caption over eyeline",                               
      1357 +     "loudness target missing", "graphic on screen > 2.5s hid
           +es the speaker") - surfaced to                               
      1358 +     Simulation/QA and the user, not necessarily fatal.      
      1359 +   - Optimization pass: deduplicate identical operations, hoi
           +st shared sub-renders, choose                                
      1360 +     proxy vs full per target, pick GPU vs CPU paths, and sel
           +ect cacheable boundaries.                                    
      1361 +   - Scheduling pass: topologically order the operations into
           + the execution DAG, grouping by                              
      1362 +     resource (GPU/CPU) and parallelizable independent branch
           +es (Section 14).                                             
      1363 +                                                             
      1364 + 12.6  Code generation - the execution DAG                   
      1365 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1366 +   Codegen lowers the optimized IR into a directed acyclic gr
           +aph of concrete, content-addressed                           
      1367 +   tool invocations (the "object code"):                     
      1368 +     nodes  = a typed tool call (ffmpeg filtergraph, remotion
           + render, loudnorm pass, composite)                           
      1369 +              with fully-resolved inputs and a deterministic 
           +cache key (hash of op + inputs + params)                     
      1370 +     edges  = data dependencies (a node consumes another node
           +'s output)                                                   
      1371 +   The DAG is the executable artifact the scheduler runs (Sec
           +tion 14). Because nodes are                                  
      1372 +   content-addressed, unchanged nodes are served from cache. 
      1373 +                                                             
      1374 + 12.7  Incremental compilation and caching                   
      1375 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1376 +   - A change to the EDD recompiles only the affected subtree
           +; nodes whose cache key is unchanged                         
      1377 +     are reused. Changing one caption style re-renders only t
           +he caption track, not the a-roll                             
      1378 +     (Goal T3, success criterion).                           
      1379 +   - The cache is content-addressed (Section 14): same op + s
           +ame inputs + same params -> same key                         
      1380 +     -> reuse. Asset hashing (Section 17) underpins this.    
      1381 +                                                             
      1382 + 12.8  Diagnostics and error model                           
      1383 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1384 +   - Every pass emits structured diagnostics with a code, sev
           +erity, the offending EDD node (with a                        
      1385 +     path), a human explanation, and (where possible) a sugge
           +sted fix - rendered in the cockpit and                       
      1386 +     consumable by agents. Tool failures are captured and cla
           +ssified (transient/fallback/fatal).                          
      1387 +                                                             
      1388 + 12.9  Why this design                                       
      1389 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1390 +   - It cleanly separates "what the user wants" (EDD) from "h
           +ow to make it" (IR/DAG), so the same                         
      1391 +     intent can target preview or final, CPU or GPU, native o
           +r fallback render, without re-asking                         
      1392 +     the model.                                              
      1393 +   - It makes edits inspectable and reversible (the AST is da
           +ta, in git).                                                 
      1394 +   - It makes rendering fast and cheap (incremental, cached).
      1395 +   - It is the well-trodden compiler architecture, applied to
           + video - reducing novelty risk.                              
      1396 +   Deep dive: docs/07-video-engine-and-compiler.md, docs/08-e
           +xecution-and-render-graph.md.                                
      1397 +                                                             
      1398  -------------------------------------------------------------
            -----------------------------------
      1122 - [END OF PART 2 - continues with Section 10: Installation Arc
           -hitecture]                                                   
      1399 + [END OF PART 3 - continues with Section 13: Data Models and 
           +Schemas]                                                     
      1400  -------------------------------------------------------------
            -----------------------------------

      1400 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1401 +                                                             
      1402 + 13.1  The model set                                         
      1403 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1404 + OpenVideo's durable state is a small set of typed, versioned
           +, JSON-or-markdown documents living                          
      1405 + in the project workspace (Section 17). All are inspectable a
           +nd git-versioned. Full JSON Schemas                          
      1406 + are in Appendix D and docs/10-data-models.md; this section g
           +ives the authoritative shapes.                               
      1407 +                                                             
      1408 +   Model            File (per project)              Role     
      1409 +   ---------------  ------------------------------   --------
           +------------------------------------

           +, dimensions, platform, refs

           +, declaratively (the AST)                                    
      1412 +   Transcript       transcripts/<asset>.json         ASR text
           + + segment/word timings                                      
      1413 +   Blueprint/Plan   plans/<id>.plan.json             approved
           + creative blueprint

           +ok system (open-design analog)

           + content hashes + probe metadata

           +addressed render-node cache                                  
      1417 +   Memory           memory/*.md                       agent/p
           +roject memory facts                                          
      1418 +   Render record    renders/<id>.json                provenan
           +ce: EDD ver, tool vers, outputs                              
      1419 +

      1477 +   Notes: punchIn, color spec, and caption style are intent-l
           +evel; lowering (Section 12.4) resolves                       
      1478 +   them to concrete keyframes/values via STYLE.md. Every node
           + can carry provenance.                                       
      1479 +                                                             
      1480 + 13.3  Project manifest (project.json)                       
      1481 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1482 +   { "id": "prj_<uuid>", "name": "...", "createdAt": "...", "
           +platform": "instagram_reel",                                 
      1483 +     "width": 1080, "height": 1920, "fps": 60, "styleRef": "S
           +TYLE.md",                                                    
      1484 +     "currentEdd": "timelines/main.edd.json", "assets": "asse
           +ts/manifest.json" }                                          
      1485 +                                                             
      1486 + 13.4  Transcript model                                      
      1487 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1488 +   { "asset": "src_1", "language": "hi+en", "model": "whisper
           +-large-v3", "device": "cuda",                                
      1489 +     "authoritative": true,                                  
      1490 +     "segments": [ { "startS": 0.0, "endS": 6.2, "text": "...
           +", "words": [                                                
      1491 +        { "t": "...", "startS": 0.0, "endS": 0.2, "conf": 0.9
           +7 } ] } ] }                                                  
      1492 +   The authoritative transcript may override raw ASR text (Po
           +C F4); romanization is applied by the                        
      1493 +   Caption agent while preserving timings (PoC F5).          
      1494 +                                                             
      1495 + 13.5  Blueprint / plan model (plans/<id>.plan.json)         
      1496 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1497 +   A structured, approvable creative plan: { spine, sections[
           +] (timestamp, line, camera, zoom,                            
      1498 +   transition, overlays, captions, sfx, broll, color), hookPl
           +an, brollList, graphicsList,                                 
      1499 +   captionStyle, audioPlan, colorPlan, exportTarget }. It is 
           +the human-readable precursor that the                        
      1500 +   assembly step turns into EDD patches; both are versioned. 
      1501 +                                                             
      1502 + 13.6  STYLE (look/brand) system - the open-design analog    
      1503 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1504 +   STYLE.md is OpenVideo's equivalent of open-design's DESIGN
           +.md: a per-project (or shared) file                          
      1505 +   that constrains every output. Sections: identity/voice; co
           +lor palette + accent; typography                             
      1506 +   (display + body faces); caption style (size, weight, highl
           +ight, emphasis treatment, safe                               
      1507 +   margins); motion language (eases, durations, punch-in ampl
           +itude); pacing defaults; audio                               
      1508 +   targets (LUFS); grade defaults; b-roll policy; anti-patter
           +ns ("no teal-orange", "captions off                          
      1509 +   eyeline"). It can be authored by the user, derived from a 
           +reference ("make it feel like                                
      1510 +   MagnatesMedia"), or shipped as a plugin. Lowering resolves
           + EDD style refs against it.                                  
      1511 +   (Full schema: docs/14-style-and-design-system.md.)        
      1512 +                                                             
      1513 + 13.7  Asset manifest + cache index                          
      1514 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1515 +   manifest.json: [ { "id":"src_1","path":"...","hash":"sha25
           +6:...","probe":{...},                                        
      1516 +                      "proxies":{ "preview":"cache/proxy/src_
           +1_540.mp4" } } ]                                             
      1517 +   cache/index.json: { "<cacheKey>": { "node":"...", "output"
           +:"cache/blobs/<hash>.<ext>",                                 
      1518 +                       "createdAt":"...", "toolVersions":{...
           +} } }                                                        
      1519 +   cacheKey = hash(operation + resolved-inputs + params + too
           +lVersions). (Section 14.4.)                                  
      1520 +                                                             
      1521 + 13.8  Versioning                                            
      1522 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1523 +   - Every model carries a schemaVersion; migrations are expl
           +icit.                                                        
      1524 +   - The EDD, transcript, plan, and STYLE are git-committed o
           +n each applied change; an "edit" is a                        
      1525 +     commit, enabling diff, blame, rollback, and reproducibil
           +ity.                                                         
      1526 +   Deep dive: docs/10-data-models.md, Appendix D.            
      1527 +                                                             
      1528 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1529 + 14. EXECUTION GRAPH, SCHEDULING, AND CACHING                
      1530 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1531 +                                                             
      1532 + 14.1  The execution DAG (recap + detail)                    
      1533 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1534 +   Codegen (Section 12.6) produces a DAG of content-addressed
           + tool-invocation nodes. Example node:                        
      1535 +     { "id":"n_grade", "op":"tonemap_grade",                 
      1536 +       "inputs":["src_1"], "params":{ "tonemap":"hlg_to_bt709
           +", ... },                                                    
      1537 +       "key":"sha256:<op+inputs+params+toolvers>", "resource"
           +:"gpu|cpu",                                                  
      1538 +       "outputs":["cache/blobs/<hash>.mp4"] }                
      1539 +   Edges encode data dependencies (composite depends on grade
           + + captions + audio). The DAG is the                         
      1540 +   single source of truth for what must run and in what order
           +.                                                            
      1541 +                                                             
      1542 + 14.2  Scheduler                                             
      1543 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1544 +   - Topologically orders nodes; runs independent branches in
           + parallel (e.g. grade a-roll while                           
      1545 +     rendering caption PNGs while leveling audio).           
      1546 +   - Resource-aware: separates GPU-bound (NVENC/CUDA), CPU-bo
           +und (libx264, filtergraphs), and                             
      1547 +     Chrome-bound (Remotion) work; sizes pools to the detecte
           +d hardware (Section 22).                                     
      1548 +   - Honors a usage/cost budget and preview-vs-final quality 
           +(Optimization agent input).                                  
      1549 +                                                             
      1550 + 14.3  Render queue and background workers                   
      1551 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1552 +   - Jobs are subgraphs submitted to a bounded worker pool; p
           +rogress (phase, %, ETA) streams to                           
      1553 +     the cockpit; jobs are cancellable; the queue applies bac
           +kpressure to avoid thrashing.                                
      1554 +   - Long jobs run in the background and notify on completion
           + (PoC F9: users want "alive" status).                        
      1555 +                                                             
      1556 + 14.4  Content-addressed cache                               
      1557 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1558 +   - Each node's output is stored under its cacheKey. Re-runn
           +ing with an unchanged key returns the                        
      1559 +     cached blob instantly. Asset hashing + resolved params +
           + pinned tool versions make keys exact.                       
      1560 +   - Cache is per-project (with an optional shared global cac
           +he for common operations); eviction is                       
      1561 +     LRU within a size budget; integrity is verified on read.
      1562 +                                                             
      1563 + 14.5  Incremental rendering                                 
      1564 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1565 +   - Changing the EDD recompiles only the affected subtree; u
           +nchanged nodes hit the cache. Changing                       
      1566 +     a caption color re-renders the caption track and the fin
           +al composite only - not the grade or                         
      1567 +     audio. This delivers the "small change = fast re-render"
           + success criterion (Goal T3).                                
      1568 +                                                             
      1569 + 14.6  Proxy generation                                      
      1570 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1571 +   - On ingest (or lazily), the engine generates low-res prox
           +ies for fast preview and QA; final                           
      1572 +     render uses full-res sources. The IR is resolution-indep
           +endent so the same graph drives both.                        
      1573 +                                                             
      1574 + 14.7  Cancellation, progress, ETA, journaling               
      1575 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1576 +   - Nodes are killable; partial outputs are discarded (never
           + half-written into cache).                                   
      1577 +   - The scheduler journals node state (queued/running/done/f
           +ailed) so a crash mid-render resumes                         
      1578 +     from the last completed nodes rather than restarting (Se
           +ction 24, 25).                                               
      1579 +                                                             
      1580 + 14.8  Failure and fallback in execution                     
      1581 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1582 +   - A node failure is classified: transient (retry with back
           +off), fallback-eligible (e.g. native                         
      1583 +     Remotion compositor -> PNG-sequence + FFmpeg; GPU encode
           + -> CPU encode), or fatal (surface a                         
      1584 +     precise diagnostic and stop the affected branch).       
      1585 +   Deep dive: docs/08-execution-and-render-graph.md.         
      1586 +                                                             
      1587 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1588 + 15. RENDERING ENGINE                                        
      1589 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1590 +                                                             
      1591 + 15.1  Two substrates, one composite model                   
      1592 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1593 + The render engine combines two deterministic substrates:    
      1594 +   - FFmpeg/FFprobe: the media workhorse - decode, cut/trim, 
           +crop/scale/position, speed, concat,                          
      1595 +     overlay, color (zscale/tonemap, curves, colorbalance), d
           +enoise (afftdn), loudness (two-pass                          
      1596 +     loudnorm), limiter, encode (libx264/NVENC), mux, faststa
           +rt, inspection.                                              
      1597 +   - Remotion (headless Chrome): declarative React components
           + for captions, lower-thirds, kinetic                         
      1598 +     headlines, comparison cards, flow diagrams, timelines, C
           +TAs, and vector b-roll - deterministic                       
      1599 +     frames driven by EDD-resolved props.                    
      1600 + The composite model: render graphics/captions as a transpare
           +nt layer (PNG sequence or MP4 with                           
      1601 + alpha), then composite over the graded, cut a-roll with FFmp
           +eg, then mux the final audio mix. This                       
      1602 + is exactly the path the proof-of-concept shipped.           
      1603 +                                                             
      1604 + 15.2  Native vs PNG-sequence render path (ADR-0006)         
      1605 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1606 + The PoC proved that Remotion's native compositor binary can 
           +fail on a given Windows machine. The                         
      1607 + engine therefore supports BOTH and selects automatically:   
      1608 +   - HEALTH CHECK at install/first-use: probe the Remotion co
           +mpositor binary (the PoC's failure                           
      1609 +     was the bundled Rust/ffprobe binary crashing on any inpu
           +t). If healthy, use the native render.                       
      1610 +   - FALLBACK: render the graphics/captions as a transparent 
           +PNG sequence via headless Chrome                             
      1611 +     (which works even when the compositor binary does not), 
           +then composite with the system FFmpeg.                       
      1612 +   - The selection is cached in the hardware/capability profi
           +le and can be forced via settings.                           
      1613 + This makes the render engine robust to the single most disru
           +ptive failure the PoC encountered.                           
      1614 +                                                             
      1615 + 15.3  FFmpeg responsibilities (typed, not raw shell)        
      1616 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1617 +   - Cutting/assembly: trim, concat, segment; smart-cut from 
           +the EDD's clip in/out points.                                
      1618 +   - Spatial: crop, scale, position, the alternating "breathe
           +" punch-in (computed zoom curve).                            
      1619 +   - Color: HLG/HDR -> Rec.709 SDR tonemap (zscale=t=linear,n
           +pl=...,tonemap=hable,...), white                             
      1620 +     balance, S-curve contrast, vibrance/saturation, light un
           +sharp, optional vignette; preserve or                        
      1621 +     set correct color tags. (PoC F7.)                       
      1622 +   - Audio: high-pass, afftdn denoise, de-ess, presence EQ, c
           +ompression, two-pass loudnorm to a                           
      1623 +     target (default -14 LUFS), alimiter; music sidechain duc
           +king; SFX placement. (PoC F8.)                               
      1624 +   - Encode/mux: libx264 (CRF/preset) or NVENC; AAC; +faststa
           +rt; platform-correct pix_fmt/profile.                        
      1625 +   All FFmpeg use is via typed tool specs (Section 8.6) that 
           +construct validated filtergraphs;                            
      1626 +   agents never receive a raw FFmpeg shell.                  
      1627 +                                                             
      1628 + 15.4  Remotion responsibilities                             
      1629 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1630 +   - A bundled Remotion project (project-local) with brand-aw
           +are components driven by STYLE.md                            
      1631 +     tokens: Captions (word-level karaoke + emphasis), Hook, 
           +LowerThird, Checklist, comparison                            
      1632 +     cards, FlowDiagram, Timeline, CTA, BrandBug, and vector 
           +b-roll.                                                      
      1633 +   - The Motion agent authors component props in the EDD; the
           + engine renders them deterministically.                      
      1634 +   - Fonts are loaded via the bundled font set; emphasis/anim
           +ation use the motion language tokens.                        
      1635 +                                                             
      1636 + 15.5  GPU acceleration and CPU fallback                     
      1637 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1638 +   - Encode: NVENC (h264_nvenc/hevc_nvenc) when an NVIDIA GPU
           + is present; libx264 otherwise.                              
      1639 +   - ASR: CUDA torch when supported (30-50x faster - PoC F3);
           + CPU torch fallback.                                         
      1640 +   - Decode/scale: hardware decode where available; CPU other
           +wise.                                                        
      1641 +   - The scheduler routes GPU-eligible nodes to the GPU pool;
           + everything has a CPU path so the                            
      1642 +     product always works (T4).                              
      1643 +                                                             
      1644 + 15.6  Color, codecs, compression, HDR/SDR                   
      1645 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1646 +   - Default deliverable: Rec.709 SDR (tonemapped from HLG/HD
           +R sources) for phone-consistent color.                       
      1647 +   - HDR passthrough/export is a roadmap option for platforms
           + that support it.                                            
      1648 +   - Codecs: H.264 (default, max compatibility), HEVC (option
           +al), with platform presets (IG/TikTok/                       
      1649 +     Shorts) controlling resolution, fps, bitrate/CRF, profil
           +e, faststart.                                                
      1650 +   - Compression: the Optimization agent targets platform siz
           +e/bitrate norms without visible loss.                        
      1651 +                                                             
      1652 + 15.7  Preview vs final                                      
      1653 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1654 +   - Preview: proxy resolution, fast preset, possibly partial
           + range, for the sandboxed preview and                        
      1655 +     QA loop; cached aggressively.                           
      1656 +   - Final: full resolution, high quality (e.g. CRF 18, slow 
           +preset), verified (ffprobe + loudness).                      
      1657 +                                                             
      1658 + 15.8  Sync, caption timing, motion interpolation            
      1659 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1660 +   - Frame-accurate sync between a-roll, captions, graphics, 
           +and audio is enforced by the IR's                            
      1661 +     normalized time base; caption word timing is honored to 
           +<= 80 ms; head-trims are applied                             
      1662 +     consistently to video and audio (the PoC's 0.5s lead-in 
           +trim is a worked example).                                   
      1663 +   - Motion (punch-ins, graphic entrances) uses eased interpo
           +lation from the motion language;                             
      1664 +     optional frame interpolation is a roadmap item.         
      1665 +                                                             
      1666 + 15.9  Output targets                                        
      1667 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1668 +   - Platform presets encode the known-good settings (e.g. IG
           + Reel: 1080x1920, 60fps, H.264 High,                         
      1669 +     AAC 48k, +faststart, ~-14 LUFS). New presets ship as dat
           +a/plugins.                                                   
      1670 +   Deep dive: docs/09-rendering-engine.md, Appendix B (ffmpeg
           + recipes from the PoC).                                      
      1671 +                                                             
      1672 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1673 + 16. PROMPT AND INTENT ENGINE                                
      1674 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1675 +                                                             
      1676 + 16.1  Intent taxonomy                                       
      1677 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1678 + The Intent Engine classifies a user utterance into a typed i
           +ntent + parameters. Top-level intent                         
      1679 + families:                                                   
      1680 +   create   (make a reel/short/clip; from footage + goal + pl
           +atform)                                                      
      1681 +   transform(re-grade, re-level, recompose, change pacing, ch
           +ange aspect)                                                 
      1682 +   analyze  (find dead frames, list cuts, measure loudness, t
           +ranscribe)                                                   
      1683 +   captions (add/edit captions; style; language/romanization;
           + emphasis)                                                   
      1684 +   broll    (generate/place b-roll)                          
      1685 +   audio    (level, denoise, music, sfx, swap audio)         
      1686 +   hook     (rebuild the opening; first-3-seconds)           
      1687 +   export   (platform-optimized deliverable)                 
      1688 +   style    (apply/derive a look system; "make it feel like X
           +")                                                           
      1689 +   project  (manage assets, versions, settings)              
      1690 +   system   (install/prepare; doctor; configure)             
      1691 + Each intent has a parameter schema and maps to a Director pl
           +aybook (which agents, in what order).                        
      1692 +                                                             
      1693 + 16.2  Intent parsing and resolution                         
      1694 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1695 +   - Resolve context: "this clip" -> the dropped/active asset
           +; "the hook" -> the opening of the                           
      1696 +     current EDD; "make it shorter" -> a constraint on the cu
           +rrent timeline.                                              
      1697 +   - Extract parameters (platform, style reference, duration 
           +constraints, language).                                      
      1698 +   - Ambiguity handling: when intent is genuinely ambiguous a
           +nd the choice materially changes the                         
      1699 +     output, ask one focused clarifying question (plan mode) 
           +rather than guessing.                                        
      1700 +                                                             
      1701 + 16.3  Prompt construction (caching-friendly)                
      1702 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1703 +   The daemon builds the CLI prompt/context in a stable, cach
           +e-friendly order (Section 22):                               
      1704 +     1. Stable system prompt (Director role, rules, tool cont
           +ract) - frozen.                                              
      1705 +     2. The project STYLE.md (changes rarely).               
      1706 +     3. The deterministic MCP tool list (sorted).            
      1707 +     4. The current EDD + analysis summaries (per-session).  
      1708 +     5. The user's latest intent (volatile, last).           
      1709 +   Stable content first preserves the prompt cache across tur
           +ns; volatile content (the new request,                       
      1710 +   timestamps) goes last. Subagents receive only their releva
           +nt slice.                                                    
      1711 +                                                             
      1712 + 16.4  Claude CLI invocation and event protocol              
      1713 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1714 +   - Spawn: claude -p "<prompt>" --output-format stream-json 
           +--input-format stream-json                                   
      1715 +            [--resume <sessionId>] [--model <id>] [effort/per
           +mission flags] [--mcp-config ...]                            
      1716 +   - Parse streamed events: thinking, tool_use, tool_result, 
           +usage, result; map them to cockpit                           
      1717 +     events (Section 19). A versioned adapter isolates the co
           +debase from CLI schema changes.                              
      1718 +   - Sessions: one per cockpit conversation; resumable; inter
           +ruptible.                                                    
      1719 +   (Full event schema + adapter contract: Appendix C; docs/11
           +-prompt-and-intent-engine.md.)                               
      1720 +                                                             
      1721 + 16.5  Plan / auto modes and permissions                     
      1722 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1723 +   - Plan mode: the Director proposes a blueprint and waits f
           +or approval before executing                                 
      1724 +     (mirrors Claude Code plan mode and the PoC's blueprint s
           +tep). Default for large operations.                          
      1725 +   - Auto mode: execute end to end with bounded autonomy, pau
           +sing only for gated actions.                                 
      1726 +   - Permission system: hard-to-reverse actions (overwriting 
           +a deliverable, network import,                               
      1727 +     installing software, deleting assets) are gated per the 
           +permission mode; the cockpit renders                         
      1728 +     approval prompts.                                       
      1729 +                                                             
      1730 + 16.6  Memory                                                
      1731 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1732 +   - Session memory (CLI transcript, compacted), project memo
           +ry (memory/*.md: style decisions,                            
      1733 +     prior critiques, user preferences), and artifact memory 
           +(versioned EDD/plan/transcript). The                         
      1734 +     Director consults project memory to stay consistent acro
           +ss sessions.                                                 
      1735 +                                                             
      1736 + 16.7  Cost and effort control                               
      1737 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1738 +   - Model + effort are user-set (control surface) and per-ag
           +ent-defaulted (Section 9.9).                                 
      1739 +   - Prompt caching, cheap-model subagents, bounded turns/eff
           +ort, and a usage meter keep cost                             
      1740 +     visible and controlled (Section 22). The usage/limit sur
           +face from the CLI is shown live.                             
      1741 +   Deep dive: docs/11-prompt-and-intent-engine.md, Appendix C
           +.                                                            
      1742 +                                                             
      1743  -------------------------------------------------------------
            -----------------------------------

           -Schemas]                                                     
      1744 + [END OF PART 4 - continues with Section 17: Workspace Design
           + and File Structure]
