      1744 + 17. WORKSPACE DESIGN AND FILE STRUCTURE                     
      1745 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1746 +                                                             
      1747 + 17.1  Application-level layout (per machine / per user)     
      1748 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1749 +   <install dir>/                      the Electron app, daem
           +on, bundled tools (ffmpeg, node,                             
      1750 +                                       python+torch toolchain
           +, Remotion runtime), MCP server                              
      1751 +   <user data dir>/OpenVideo/                                
      1752 +     config/                           app settings, hardware
           +/capability profile, control defaults                        
      1753 +     secrets/                          encrypted credentials/
           +keystore (Section 23)                                        
      1754 +     models/                           downloaded model weigh
           +ts (Whisper, optional packs) - shared                        
      1755 +     cache-global/                     content-addressed cach
           +e shared across projects (optional)                          
      1756 +     plugins/                          installed plugins (age
           +nts, styles, templates, renderers)                           
      1757 +     logs/                             app + daemon logs, dia
           +gnostics                                                     
      1758 +     projects/                         all user projects (eac
           +h is a self-contained dir below)                             
      1759 +                                                             
      1760 + 17.2  Per-project layout (self-contained, portable, git-back
           +ed)                                                          
      1761 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1762 +   projects/<project>/                                       
      1763 +     project.json        identity + dimensions + platform + r
           +efs (Section 13.3)                                           
      1764 +     STYLE.md            the look/brand system constraining o
           +utputs (Section 13.6, 14-doc)                                
      1765 +     assets/             imported source media + manifest.jso
           +n (hashes + probe)         [INPUT]                           
      1766 +     downloads/          sandboxed imports (yt-dlp) before pr
           +omotion to assets/         [INPUT]                           
      1767 +     transcripts/        ASR transcripts + timings (authorita
           +tive)                      [DERIVED]                         
      1768 +     plans/              approved creative blueprints (versio
           +ned)                       [PLAN]                            
      1769 +     timelines/          the EDD(s) - the Video AST(s) (the h
           +eart; git-versioned)       [AST]                             
      1770 +     agents/             project-local agent/subagent definit
           +ions + overrides           [CONFIG]                          
      1771 +     prompts/            saved prompts / prompt history for t
           +his project                [HISTORY]                         
      1772 +     memory/             project memory (style decisions, cri
           +tiques, preferences)       [MEMORY]                          
      1773 +     plugins/            project-local plugins (in addition t
           +o global)                  [EXT]                             
      1774 +     models/             project-pinned model references (usu
           +ally link to shared)       [REF]                             
      1775 +     cache/              content-addressed render-node cache 
           ++ proxies + index.json     [CACHE]                           
      1776 +     renders/            intermediate + preview renders + ren
           +der records (provenance)   [OUTPUT]                          
      1777 +     exports/            final platform-optimized deliverable
           +s                          [OUTPUT]                          
      1778 +     versions/           tagged snapshots / named versions of
           + the edit                  [HISTORY]                         
      1779 +     backups/            periodic safety backups of project s
           +tate                       [SAFETY]                          
      1780 +     logs/               per-project logs                    
           +                           [OPS]                             
      1781 +                                                             
      1782 +   Purpose of each directory:                                
      1783 +     assets/      authoritative source media; never mutated; 
           +everything derives from here.                                
      1784 +     downloads/   quarantine for fetched media pending the us
           +er's promotion (permission-gated).                           
      1785 +     transcripts/ machine-readable speech with timings; sourc
           +e of truth for captions/cuts.                                
      1786 +     plans/       the approvable creative blueprints (human-r
           +eadable + structured).                                       
      1787 +     timelines/   the EDDs - the declarative edit; the single
           + contract between agents and engine.                         
      1788 +     agents/      lets a project override or add specialized 
           +agents/skills (e.g. a house caption                          
      1789 +                  agent) without touching the app.           
      1790 +     prompts/     a searchable history of what was asked (rep
           +roducibility + reuse).                                       
      1791 +     memory/      durable facts the agents consult across ses
           +sions (consistency).                                         
      1792 +     plugins/     project-scoped extensions (a client-specifi
           +c look pack, say).                                           
      1793 +     models/      pins which model weights/versions this proj
           +ect expects (reproducibility).                               
      1794 +     cache/       makes re-rendering incremental and fast; sa
           +fe to delete (regenerable).                                  
      1795 +     renders/     work product + provenance (which EDD/tool v
           +ersions produced what).                                      
      1796 +     exports/     the things the user actually ships.        
      1797 +     versions/    named checkpoints ("v1 sent to client", "ve
           +rtical cut") on top of git history.                          
      1798 +     backups/     belt-and-suspenders recovery independent of
           + git.                                                        
      1799 +     logs/        debugging and audit for this project's oper
           +ations.                                                      
      1800 +                                                             
      1801 + 17.3  Versioning model (git-backed)                         
      1802 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1803 +   - The project is a git repository. Each applied edit commi
           +ts the changed EDD/plan/STYLE/                               
      1804 +     transcript with a message attributing the agent and rati
           +onale (from provenance). This yields                         
      1805 +     diff, blame, rollback, branching ("try a punchier hook o
           +n a branch"), and reproducibility -                          
      1806 +     for free, using the most battle-tested versioning system
           + in existence.                                               
      1807 +   - Large binaries (assets, renders, cache) are git-ignored 
           +or tracked via LFS-style pointers;                           
      1808 +     the durable, versioned state is the small JSON/markdown 
           +(EDD/plan/STYLE/transcript) plus                             
      1809 +     content hashes that tie commits to specific media.      
      1810 +   - "versions/" provides human-named snapshots layered on co
           +mmits for non-technical recall.                              
      1811 +                                                             
      1812 + 17.4  Asset management and hashing                          
      1813 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1814 +   - On import, each asset is content-hashed (sha256) and pro
           +bed; the hash is the identity used in                        
      1815 +     the EDD and cache keys, so identical media is deduplicat
           +ed and renders are reproducible.                             
      1816 +   - Proxies live in cache/ keyed off the source hash; deleti
           +ng cache/ never loses real data.                             
      1817 +                                                             
      1818 + 17.5  Portability                                           
      1819 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1820 +   - A project directory is self-contained (assets + EDD + st
           +yle + history). Zipping/cloning it                           
      1821 +     moves the entire reproducible edit. Cache/renders are re
           +generable and need not travel.                               
      1822 +   Deep dive: docs/12-workspace-and-file-structure.md.       
      1823 +                                                             
      1824 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1825 + 18. USER EXPERIENCE (UX)                                    
      1826 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1827 +                                                             
      1828 + 18.1  The cockpit at a glance                               
      1829 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1830 +   A calm, premium, keyboard-first desktop app. Default layou
           +t (resizable, dockable):                                     
      1831 +                                                             
      1832 +     +-------------------+-----------------------------------
           +--------+--------------------+                               
      1833 +     | Projects / Assets |  Conversation (chat)              
           +        |  Preview           |                               
      1834 +     | (left rail)       |  - user intent + agent responses  
           +        |  (sandboxed iframe:|                               
      1835 +     |                   |  - plan proposals (approve/amend) 
           +        |   Remotion/render) |                               
      1836 +     |                   |  - inline approvals (permissions) 
           +        |  + EDD inspector/  |                               
      1837 +     |                   |-----------------------------------
           +--------|    diff viewer     |                               
      1838 +     |                   |  Live "alive" Terminal            
           +        |                    |                               
      1839 +     |                   |  Thinking... Analyzing footage... 
           +        |  Render queue +    |                               
      1840 +     |                   |  Detecting silence... Rendering ca
           +ptions  |  progress          |                               
      1841 +     +-------------------+-----------------------------------
           +--------+--------------------+                               
      1842 +     | Control surface (bottom bar): model [Opus|Sonnet|Haiku
           +]  effort [low..max]         |                               
      1843 +     |   mode [plan|auto]  permissions [...]   |   Usage/limi
           +ts meter [#####----]          |                              
      1844 +     +-------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------+                              
      1845 +                                                             
      1846 + 18.2  The control surface                                   
      1847 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1848 +   - Model picker: Opus (claude-opus-4-8, default/quality), S
           +onnet (claude-sonnet-4-6, balanced),                         
      1849 +     Haiku (claude-haiku-4-5, fast/cheap). Maps directly to C
           +LI --model.                                                  
      1850 +   - Effort: low / medium / high / xhigh / max (maps to CLI e
           +ffort). A global "fast vs max quality"                       
      1851 +     bias the Director propagates to subagents (Section 9.9).
      1852 +   - Mode: plan (propose-then-approve) vs auto (bounded auton
           +omy). Maps to plan/permission flags.                         
      1853 +   - Permissions: per-category gating of hard-to-reverse acti
           +ons (render-overwrite, import,                               
      1854 +     install, delete) with inline approval prompts.          
      1855 +   These are exactly the controls the user envisioned ("OPUS 
           +or SONNET, high low medium xhigh ...                         
      1856 +   plan mode, auto mode") and they are first-class, not burie
           +d in settings.                                               
      1857 +                                                             
      1858 + 18.3  Usage and limits meter                                
      1859 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1860 +   - A live meter shows token/cost usage for the session and 
           +progress toward the user's Claude                            
      1861 +     plan limits (parsed from the CLI's usage events), with a
           + clear "approaching limit" warning -                         
      1862 +     the user's explicit request. (Section 22 details how usa
           +ge is sourced and surfaced.)                                 
      1863 +                                                             
      1864 + 18.4  Media drop and workspace                              
      1865 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1866 +   - Drag-drop a clip anywhere to import it into the active p
           +roject (or create one). The left rail                        
      1867 +     browses projects and assets; selecting an asset scopes "
           +this clip" for intent resolution.                            
      1868 +                                                             
      1869 + 18.5  Preview and EDD inspector                             
      1870 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1871 +   - The preview pane shows the rendered result in a sandboxe
           +d iframe (open-design pattern).                              
      1872 +   - The EDD inspector renders the Video AST as a navigable t
           +ree with provenance ("why is this                            
      1873 +     here?") and a diff view across versions ("what changed w
           +hen I asked for a punchier hook?").                          
      1874 +     This is how "every edit is explainable/inspectable" beco
           +mes tangible UX.                                             
      1875 +                                                             
      1876 + 18.6  The canonical interaction (the experience the product 
           +promises)                                                    
      1877 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1878 +   1. User opens OpenVideo. The cockpit appears; a terminal i
           +s already open.                                              
      1879 +   2. The system prepares the environment (Installation Agent
           +, tiered) with live status.                                  
      1880 +   3. User drops IMG_1554.mp4 and types: "Edit this into a pr
           +emium reel."                                                 
      1881 +   4. The terminal comes alive: Thinking... Analyzing footage
           +... Building transcript...                                   
      1882 +      Detecting silence... Finding jump cuts... Generating ti
           +meline...                                                    
      1883 +   5. In plan mode, the Director presents a blueprint; the us
           +er approves (or amends in language).                         
      1884 +   6. Execution: Generating B-roll... Rendering captions... O
           +ptimizing audio... Running FFmpeg...                         
      1885 +      Rendering preview... Validating output...              
      1886 +   7. The preview appears; QA reports it meets the bar (or pr
           +oposes fixes).                                               
      1887 +   8. The user says "ship it for Instagram"; the Export agent
           + produces and verifies the file.                             
      1888 +   No timeline was touched; no tool was installed by hand; ev
           +ery step was visible and explainable.                        
      1889 +                                                             
      1890 + 18.7  Plan-mode and approval UX                             
      1891 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1892 +   - Blueprints render as readable, structured proposals with
           + an Approve / Amend (in language) /                          
      1893 +     Reject affordance. Permission prompts are inline, specif
           +ic ("Overwrite exports/final.mp4?"),                         
      1894 +     and remembered per policy.                              
      1895 +                                                             
      1896 + 18.8  Accessibility and keyboard-first                      
      1897 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1898 +   - Full keyboard control (command palette, focus management
           +), screen-reader labels, high-contrast                       
      1899 +     and reduced-motion options, scalable type. The terminal/
           +chat is fully navigable without a mouse.                     
      1900 +                                                             
      1901 + 18.9  Design language                                       
      1902 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1903 +   - Premium, restrained, brand-aware - the open-design / Cla
           +ude Design sensibility: calm surfaces,                       
      1904 +     purposeful motion, strong typographic hierarchy, dark-fi
           +rst with a light option. The app's own                       
      1905 +     UI is itself governed by a design-token system (and the 
           +project STYLE.md governs outputs).                           
      1906 +   Deep dive: docs/13-ux-and-terminal.md, docs/14-style-and-d
           +esign-system.md.                                             
      1907 +                                                             
      1908 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1909 + 19. TERMINAL EXPERIENCE                                     
      1910 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1911 +                                                             
      1912 + 19.1  Philosophy - the terminal should feel alive           
      1913 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1914 +   The terminal is the heartbeat of the product. It must conv
           +ey momentum and intelligence without                         
      1915 +   drowning the user in raw complexity. Two layers:          
      1916 +     - The "alive" layer (default): human-legible status line
           +s that narrate what the system is                            
      1917 +       doing right now ("Analyzing footage...", "Detecting si
           +lence...", "Rendering captions...").                         
      1918 +     - The "raw" layer (on demand): the actual underlying act
           +ivity - tool invocations, ffmpeg                             
      1919 +       command lines, stderr, exit codes - for power users an
           +d debugging.                                                 
      1920 +                                                             
      1921 + 19.2  Event-to-line mapping                                 
      1922 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1923 +   Daemon/agent events map to friendly status lines:         
      1924 +     CLI thinking            -> "Thinking..."                
      1925 +     Planner running         -> "Planning the edit..."       
      1926 +     probe/transcribe        -> "Analyzing footage..." / "Bui
           +lding transcript..."                                         
      1927 +     detect_silence/cuts     -> "Detecting silence..." / "Fin
           +ding jump cuts..."                                           
      1928 +     EDD assembly            -> "Generating timeline..."     
      1929 +     B-roll agent            -> "Generating B-roll..."       
      1930 +     Remotion render         -> "Rendering captions..." / "Re
           +ndering motion graphics..."                                  
      1931 +     level_audio             -> "Optimizing audio..."        
      1932 +     ffmpeg_compose          -> "Running FFmpeg..." / "Compos
           +iting..."                                                    
      1933 +     preview render          -> "Rendering preview..."       
      1934 +     QA/Validation           -> "Validating output..."       
      1935 +     export                  -> "Exporting for Instagram..." 
      1936 +   Each line carries a phase, an optional progress bar/ETA, a
           +nd a disclosure to the raw layer.                            
      1937 +                                                             
      1938 + 19.3  Progress, background jobs, notifications              
      1939 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1940 +   - Long operations run in the background with streamed prog
           +ress and ETA; the user can keep                              
      1941 +     working or queue more. Completion raises a notification 
           +(the PoC repeatedly showed users want                        
      1942 +     this). Jobs are cancellable.                            
      1943 +                                                             
      1944 + 19.4  The connected, behind-the-scenes terminal             
      1945 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1946 +   - A real, connected terminal view (the "raw" layer) shows 
           +the actual commands and output the                           
      1947 +     daemon runs, so nothing is hidden from a user who wants 
           +to see it - matching the user's vision                       
      1948 +     of "a connected terminal open that works as behind the s
           +cenes."                                                      
      1949 +                                                             
      1950 + 19.5  Legibility rules                                      
      1951 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1952 +   - Never expose raw complexity unnecessarily; never hide it
           + when asked. Errors are translated to                        
      1953 +     plain language with a "show details" disclosure. Color/t
           +ypography keep the stream scannable.                         
      1954 +   Deep dive: docs/13-ux-and-terminal.md.                    
      1955 +                                                             
      1956 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1957 + 20. PLUGIN SDK AND ECOSYSTEM                                
      1958 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      1959 +                                                             
      1960 + 20.1  Philosophy                                            
      1961 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1962 +   Following open-design: skills, agents, styles, templates, 
           +and renderers are plain files anyone                         
      1963 +   can author, inspect, and share. The core stays small; capa
           +bility grows through plugins. This is                        
      1964 +   how OpenVideo becomes a platform, not just an app.        
      1965 +                                                             
      1966 + 20.2  Plugin types                                          
      1967 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1968 +   - Agents/Skills: new specialized agents or task playbooks 
           +(SKILL.md / agent definitions).                              
      1969 +   - Caption styles: parameterized caption looks (consumed by
           + the Caption/Motion agents).                                 
      1970 +   - Transitions: new transition types (Remotion/FFmpeg-backe
           +d).                                                          
      1971 +   - Templates: full project/blueprint templates ("60s SaaS p
           +romo", "legal explainer reel").                              
      1972 +   - Animation packs: reusable Remotion components/motion pre
           +sets.                                                        
      1973 +   - Look/Style systems: shareable STYLE.md packs ("MagnatesM
           +edia-style", a brand kit).                                   
      1974 +   - Renderers: alternative render engines (e.g. a HyperFrame
           +s signature-moment renderer).                                
      1975 +   - Music/SFX providers: royalty-safe asset sources (license
           +d integrations).                                             
      1976 +   - Importers: new media-import sources (authorized).       
      1977 +   - Cloud render: offload rendering to a configured backend 
           +(roadmap).                                                   
      1978 +                                                             
      1979 + 20.3  The manifest (openvideo.json)                         
      1980 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1981 +   { "name": "premium-captions", "version": "1.0.0", "type": 
           +"caption-style",                                             
      1982 +     "entry": "index.(ts|js|md)", "capabilities": ["edd:patch
           +","remotion:component"],                                     
      1983 +     "permissions": ["fs:project-read","fs:project-write"], "
           +params": { ... apply-time config ... },                      
      1984 +     "dependencies": [ { "tool": "ffmpeg", "min": "6.0" } ], 
      1985 +     "preview": "preview.png", "license": "Apache-2.0" }     
      1986 +   The manifest mirrors open-design's plugin spec: declared c
           +apabilities, permissions, parameters,                        
      1987 +   dependencies (which the Installation Agent provisions on t
           +he tiered basis), and preview assets.                        
      1988 +                                                             
      1989 + 20.4  Lifecycle                                             
      1990 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1991 +   discover (marketplace/registry or local) -> install (verif
           +y signature/manifest; provision                              
      1992 +   declared deps) -> load (register capabilities with the dae
           +mon/MCP) -> run (invoked by agents or                        
      1993 +   the user) -> sandbox (executed under least privilege; see 
           +20.5).                                                       
      1994 +                                                             
      1995 + 20.5  Capabilities and permissions (sandboxing)             
      1996 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      1997 +   - A plugin declares the capabilities it needs (e.g. edd:pa
           +tch, remotion:component, fs:project-                         
      1998 +     read, net:fetch); the daemon enforces them. Untrusted pl
           +ugin code runs sandboxed (worker/VM                          
      1999 +     boundary; no ambient filesystem/network); network access
           + is proxied (SSRF-guarded). High-risk                        
      2000 +     capabilities require explicit user consent. (Section 23.
           +)                                                            
      2001 +                                                             
      2002 + 20.6  Distribution                                          
      2003 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2004 +   - A community registry/marketplace (open-design model) wit
           +h manifests, previews, and one-click                         
      2005 +     install; plugins are plain folders, so they can also be 
           +shared as files or via git.                                  
      2006 +                                                             
      2007 + 20.7  Authoring (example)                                   
      2008 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2009 +   - A caption-style plugin ships a Remotion component + a ma
           +nifest + params; the Caption agent                           
      2010 +     discovers it via /capabilities and the user selects it (
           +"use the neon caption style").                               
      2011 +   Deep dive: docs/15-plugin-sdk.md.                         
      2012 +                                                             
      2013 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2014 + 21. DEVELOPER EXPERIENCE (DX)                               
      2015 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2016 +                                                             
      2017 + 21.1  Monorepo layout (pnpm)                                
      2018 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2019 +   openvideo/                                                
      2020 +     apps/                                                   
      2021 +       cockpit/        Electron + Next.js UI                 
      2022 +       daemon/         the privileged Node service (session, 
           +queue, MCP, installer, compiler)                             
      2023 +     packages/                                               
      2024 +       edd/            EDD schema + types + validation + lowe
           +ring                                                         
      2025 +       compiler/       IR + passes + DAG codegen             
      2026 +       render/         render engine (FFmpeg + Remotion adapt
           +ers, fallback logic)                                         
      2027 +       mcp-server/     the OpenVideo MCP tool surface        
      2028 +       cli-adapter/    versioned Claude CLI spawn + event par
           +ser (Appendix C)                                             
      2029 +       installer/      hardware detection + tiered provisioni
           +ng                                                           
      2030 +       agents/         bundled agent/skill definitions       
      2031 +       remotion/       bundled Remotion components (captions,
           + graphics)                                                   
      2032 +       shared/         types, protocol (Edit/Session), utils 
      2033 +     plugins/          first-party plugins (styles, templates
           +, transitions)                                               
      2034 +     docs/             this documentation set                
      2035 +     e2e/              end-to-end tests + golden fixtures    
      2036 +                                                             
      2037 + 21.2  Build and dev loop                                    
      2038 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2039 +   - pnpm workspace; one command brings up the daemon + cockp
           +it in dev (hot reload for the UI;                            
      2040 +     watch-rebuild for the daemon). A bundled, pinned toolcha
           +in (ffmpeg/node/python+torch/Remotion)                       
      2041 +     so contributors don't fight native installs (PoC lesson)
           +.                                                            
      2042 +                                                             
      2043 + 21.3  Testing locally                                       
      2044 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2045 +   - Unit tests on the EDD/compiler/IR; golden-frame render t
           +ests; an agent eval harness with                             
      2046 +     recorded fixtures so agent changes are measurable (Secti
           +on 24).                                                      
      2047 +                                                             
      2048 + 21.4  Contributing                                          
      2049 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2050 +   - Skills, agents, styles, templates, and plugins are plain
           + files - the lowest-friction                                 
      2051 +     contribution path (open-design model). Core changes go t
           +hrough the packages above with tests.                        
      2052 +                                                             
      2053 + 21.5  API stability                                         
      2054 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2055 +   - The Edit/Session protocol, the MCP tool contract, the ED
           +D schema, and the plugin manifest are                        
      2056 +     versioned with deprecation policies, so the ecosystem ca
           +n rely on them.                                              
      2057 +   Deep dive: docs/15-plugin-sdk.md, docs/04-system-architect
           +ure.md.

      2058  
      2059 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2060 + 22. PERFORMANCE ENGINEERING                                 
      2061 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2062 +                                                             
      2063 + 22.1  Performance goals                                     
      2064 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2065 +   - Responsive UI at all times (no long task blocks the even
           +t loop).                                                     
      2066 +   - Fast iteration: a small EDD change re-renders in seconds
           +, not minutes (incremental + cache).                         
      2067 +   - Exploit available hardware (GPU) but always work without
           + it (CPU fallback).                                          
      2068 +   - Predictable, visible cost and progress (usage meter, ETA
           +s).                                                          
      2069 +                                                             
      2070 + 22.2  GPU acceleration and CPU fallback                     
      2071 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2072 +   - ASR: CUDA torch (30-50x faster than CPU - PoC F3) when a
           + supported NVIDIA GPU is present;                            
      2073 +     CPU torch otherwise.                                    
      2074 +   - Encode: NVENC when present; libx264 otherwise.          
      2075 +   - Decode/scale: hardware paths where available.           
      2076 +   - The resource scheduler tags each DAG node gpu|cpu and ro
           +utes to the matching pool; the                               
      2077 +     Optimization agent decides model size and device per the
           + hardware profile and the user's                             
      2078 +     speed/quality bias. The product never silently traps a u
           +ser in a 40-minute CPU transcription                         
      2079 +     when a one-time GPU setup makes it a minute (it offers t
           +he setup).                                                   
      2080 +                                                             
      2081 + 22.3  Incremental and cached rendering                      
      2082 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2083 +   - Content-addressed cache (Section 14.4) + incremental rec
           +ompile (Section 14.5) are the primary                        
      2084 +     speed levers: unchanged DAG nodes are never recomputed. 
           +Proxies accelerate preview.                                  
      2085 +                                                             
      2086 + 22.4  Parallel execution and resource scheduling            
      2087 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2088 +   - Independent DAG branches run concurrently (grade || capt
           +ion-render || audio-level), bounded by                       
      2089 +     a pool sized to CPU cores and GPU availability, with bac
           +kpressure to prevent thrashing.                              
      2090 +   - Analysis agents fan out in parallel (Transcript || Color
           + || Audio).                                                  
      2091 +                                                             
      2092 + 22.5  Proxy and preview                                     
      2093 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2094 +   - Low-res proxies + draft encodes make preview/QA fast; fi
           +nal uses full-res from the same IR.                          
      2095 +                                                             
      2096 + 22.6  Background rendering and queue                        
      2097 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2098 +   - The render queue runs jobs off the UI thread with progre
           +ss/ETA and cancellation; completion                          
      2099 +     notifications keep the user informed (PoC F9).          
      2100 +                                                             
      2101 + 22.7  Memory optimization and large projects                
      2102 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2103 +   - Stream media through tools rather than loading wholesale
           +; reference large artifacts by path;                         
      2104 +     cap concurrent heavy operations; spill to disk for big i
           +ntermediates; lazy-load assets and                           
      2105 +     proxies. Long-form/large-project scale is a roadmap hard
           +ening target (Section 26).                                   
      2106 +                                                             
      2107 + 22.8  Agent-layer cost and latency control                  
      2108 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2109 +   - Prompt caching: stable context first (system prompt, STY
           +LE.md, sorted tool list), volatile                           
      2110 +     last - so repeated turns hit the cache (Section 16.3).  
      2111 +   - Cheap subagents: mechanical work on claude-haiku-4-5 / p
           +ure tools; reserve opus-4-8 for                              
      2112 +     judgment (Section 9.9).                                 
      2113 +   - Bounded effort/turns: the Director caps iteration; the Q
           +A loop has a budget; effort is                               
      2114 +     user-biasable.                                          
      2115 +   - Usage meter sourcing: the CLI emits usage on its events;
           + the daemon aggregates per session and                       
      2116 +     against the user's plan, surfaces a live meter, and warn
           +s near limits (user's explicit ask).                         
      2117 +                                                             
      2118 + 22.9  Distributed / cloud rendering (roadmap)               
      2119 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2120 +   - The DAG is naturally distributable: nodes are content-ad
           +dressed and independent branches can                         
      2121 +     run on remote workers. A cloud-render plugin (opt-in) ca
           +n offload heavy final renders; the                           
      2122 +     local cache stays authoritative (Section 26).           
      2123 +                                                             
      2124 + 22.10 Crash recovery                                        
      2125 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2126 +   - Journaled node state lets a render resume from completed
           + nodes after a crash (Section 24.9).                         
      2127 +   Deep dive: docs/16-performance.md.                        
      2128 +                                                             
      2129 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2130 + 23. SECURITY ARCHITECTURE                                   
      2131 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2132 +                                                             
      2133 + 23.1  Threat model (what we defend against)                 
      2134 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2135 +   - A malicious or buggy plugin attempting filesystem/networ
           +k abuse or code execution.                                   
      2136 +   - Prompt-injection via imported media/metadata/transcripts
           + steering the agent to harmful tool                          
      2137 +     calls (e.g. delete files, exfiltrate data).             
      2138 +   - SSRF via any outbound proxy (a plugin coaxing the proxy 
           +to hit internal endpoints).                                  
      2139 +   - Secret leakage (API keys, provider credentials).        
      2140 +   - Accidental destructive actions (overwriting/deleting the
           + user's work).                                               
      2141 +   - Supply-chain compromise of bundled tools/dependencies.  
      2142 +                                                             
      2143 + 23.2  Privilege model                                       
      2144 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2145 +   - The daemon is the ONLY privileged process: it alone touc
           +hes the filesystem, spawns processes,                        
      2146 +     and reaches the network. The renderer is sandboxed (cont
           +extIsolation on, nodeIntegration off);                       
      2147 +     it acts only through a typed preload bridge to the daemo
           +n. (Open-design model.)                                      
      2148 +   - This single-privileged-process design contains blast rad
           +ius: a compromised renderer or plugin                        
      2149 +     cannot directly act on the system.                      
      2150 +                                                             
      2151 + 23.3  Tool sandboxing                                       
      2152 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2153 +   - Media tools run as child processes with constrained argu
           +ments (typed tool specs, never raw                           
      2154 +     model-authored shell for privileged actions), captured o
           +utput, timeouts, working directory                           
      2155 +     pinned to the project sandbox, and no inherited secrets.
      2156 +   - A constrained bash tool MAY exist for breadth, but hard-
           +to-reverse actions are promoted to                           
      2157 +     dedicated, gated tools (the agent-design principle), so 
           +the harness can intercept/audit them.                        
      2158 +                                                             
      2159 + 23.4  Plugin sandboxing and permissions                     
      2160 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2161 +   - Untrusted plugin code runs under least privilege (worker
           +/VM boundary, no ambient fs/net).                            
      2162 +   - Plugins declare capabilities/permissions in the manifest
           +; the daemon enforces them; high-risk                        
      2163 +     capabilities require explicit user consent; network goes
           + through the SSRF-guarded proxy.                             
      2164 +                                                             
      2165 + 23.5  Permission system                                     
      2166 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2167 +   - Hard-to-reverse actions (overwrite a deliverable, delete
           + assets, network import, install                             
      2168 +     software, run a plugin's privileged capability) are gate
           +d per the permission mode; the cockpit                       
      2169 +     renders specific, inline approval prompts and remembers 
           +per-policy decisions. Mirrors Claude                         
      2170 +     Code's permission modes.                                
      2171 +                                                             
      2172 + 23.6  Secrets and credential storage                        
      2173 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2174 +   - Secrets (e.g. provider API keys for optional plugins) ar
           +e stored in an OS-keychain-backed,                           
      2175 +     encrypted keystore - never in the EDD, prompts, logs, or
           + project files. They are injected by                         
      2176 +     the daemon at call time, not exposed to the renderer, ag
           +ents, or plugin sandboxes.                                   
      2177 +   - The Claude CLI uses the user's existing subscription aut
           +h managed by the CLI itself; OpenVideo                       
      2178 +     does not store the user's Claude credentials.           
      2179 +                                                             
      2180 + 23.7  Network permissions and the SSRF-guarded proxy        
      2181 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2182 +   - Default posture is offline. Any outbound request (model-
           +weight download, authorized import,                          
      2183 +     plugin provider call) goes through the daemon's proxy wi
           +th SSRF protection (block private/loop                       
      2184 +     back/link-local ranges, validate redirects, allowlist ho
           +sts where possible) - the open-design                        
      2185 +     BYOK-proxy pattern.                                     
      2186 +                                                             
      2187 + 23.8  Filesystem protection                                 
      2188 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2189 +   - All file operations are validated against the project sa
           +ndbox (path normalization, no                                
      2190 +     traversal, no symlink escape). The daemon refuses writes
           + outside the project/app data dirs.                          
      2191 +   - Before any overwrite/delete, the target is inspected and
           + the action gated (Section 23.5).                            
      2192 +                                                             
      2193 + 23.9  Supply chain                                          
      2194 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2195 +   - Bundled tools and dependencies are pinned and integrity-
           +checked; plugins carry manifests and                         
      2196 +     (where distributed via the registry) signatures verified
           + on install.                                                 
      2197 +                                                             
      2198 + 23.10 Privacy (local-first)                                 
      2199 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2200 +   - Footage and project data never leave the machine unless 
           +the user explicitly opts into a                              
      2201 +     networked feature. Telemetry is opt-in and never include
           +s media content. This is decisive for                        
      2202 +     creators handling unreleased/sensitive material.        
      2203 +   Deep dive: docs/17-security.md.                           
      2204 +                                                             
      2205 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2206 + 24. TESTING AND QUALITY ASSURANCE                           
      2207 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2208 +                                                             
      2209 + 24.1  Strategy                                              
      2210 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2211 +   A layered strategy that treats both deterministic code (co
           +mpiler/render) and non-deterministic                         
      2212 +   agents as testable, plus product-level QA of the actual vi
           +deo output.                                                  
      2213 +                                                             
      2214 + 24.2  Unit tests (deterministic core)                       
      2215 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2216 +   - EDD schema validation; lowering (EDD -> IR) correctness;
           + each compiler pass (validation, lint,                       
      2217 +     optimization, scheduling); cache-key computation; protoc
           +ol (Edit/Session) encoding.                                  
      2218 +                                                             
      2219 + 24.3  Golden-frame render tests                             
      2220 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2221 +   - Fixed EDD + assets -> render -> compare frames/loudness/
           +format against committed golden                              
      2222 +     outputs (within tolerance, encoder non-determinism pinne
           +d). Catches regressions in grade,                            
      2223 +     captions, composite, and export.                        
      2224 +                                                             
      2225 + 24.4  Integration tests (pipeline)                          
      2226 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2227 +   - Run real tool chains (probe/transcribe/grade/level/compo
           +se) on small fixtures across the                             
      2228 +     native and PNG-sequence render paths, and across GPU/CPU
           + paths where the CI agent allows.                            
      2229 +                                                             
      2230 + 24.5  End-to-end tests                                      
      2231 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2232 +   - Drive the cockpit -> daemon -> (stubbed or recorded) age
           +nt -> render, asserting the canonical                        
      2233 +     interaction (Section 18.6) produces a valid deliverable.
      2234 +                                                             
      2235 + 24.6  Agent evaluation harness                              
      2236 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2237 +   - Recorded fixtures (intent + footage analysis) run throug
           +h the agents with assertions on the                          
      2238 +     produced EDD (e.g. "hook within first 1.5s", "caption sy
           +nc <= 80ms", "loudness target set",                          
      2239 +     "no static frame > 4s"). Lets agent/prompt changes be me
           +asured, not guessed. A rubric-based                          
      2240 +     QA-agent self-eval complements human spot checks.       
      2241 +                                                             
      2242 + 24.7  Determinism tests                                     
      2243 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2244 +   - Same EDD + assets + tool versions -> same output hash (v
           +ideo stream) within pinned tolerance.                        
      2245 +                                                             
      2246 + 24.8  Performance / regression tests                        
      2247 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2248 +   - Track render time and incremental re-render time on benc
           +hmark projects; flag regressions; verify                     
      2249 +     "change one caption -> only caption track re-renders".  
      2250 +                                                             
      2251 + 24.9  Crash and recovery tests                              
      2252 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2253 +   - Kill the app/daemon mid-render and assert: no corrupted 
           +cache, committed EDD intact, render                          
      2254 +     resumes from journaled state or restarts cleanly.       
      2255 +                                                             
      2256 + 24.10 CI                                                    
      2257 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2258 +   - Windows-first CI runners (matching ADR-0007) run unit/in
           +tegration/golden/e2e; agent evals run                        
      2259 +     on a schedule (cost-aware). Deep dive: docs/18-testing-a
           +nd-qa.md.                                                    
      2260 +                                                             
      2261 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2262 + 25. DEPLOYMENT, PACKAGING, AND RELEASE                      
      2263 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2264 +                                                             
      2265 + 25.1  Packaging                                             
      2266 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2267 +   - electron-builder produces a Windows installer (first), b
           +undling the cockpit, the daemon, and a                       
      2268 +     pinned core toolchain (ffmpeg/ffprobe, node/pnpm, Remoti
           +on runtime) plus the bundled Python +                        
      2269 +     torch toolchain stub; heavy items (model weights, CUDA) 
           +are fetched by the Installation Agent                        
      2270 +     on the tiered basis (ADR-0004). macOS/Linux packaging fo
           +llows (ADR-0007).                                            
      2271 +                                                             
      2272 + 25.2  Channels                                              
      2273 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2274 +   - stable / beta / nightly channels; pinned dependency sets
           + per release for reproducibility.                            
      2275 +                                                             
      2276 + 25.3  Auto-update                                           
      2277 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2278 +   - Background, signed auto-update for the app; the Installa
           +tion Agent handles tool/model upgrades                       
      2279 +     with verification and rollback (Section 10.8).          
      2280 +                                                             
      2281 + 25.4  Telemetry (opt-in)                                    
      2282 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2283 +   - Strictly opt-in, privacy-preserving (no media, no projec
           +t content): crash signals, anonymized                        
      2284 +     performance metrics, feature usage - to guide engineerin
           +g. Off by default.                                           
      2285 +                                                             
      2286 + 25.5  Diagnostics / doctor                                  
      2287 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2288 +   - A "doctor" command re-profiles hardware, verifies the to
           +olchain, health-checks the Remotion                          
      2289 +     compositor, and self-heals (re-install/repair) - turning
           + the PoC's manual debugging into a                           
      2290 +     one-click flow.                                         
      2291 +                                                             
      2292 + 25.6  Crash reporting and recovery                          
      2293 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2294 +   - Local crash logs + (opt-in) crash reports; journaled sta
           +te enables resume-after-crash for                            
      2295 +     renders and preserves project integrity (Section 24.9). 
      2296 +                                                             
      2297 + 25.7  Release process                                       
      2298 + ------------------------------------------------------------
           +------------------------------------                         
      2299 +   - Versioned releases with changelogs; schema/protocol/mani
           +fest versions and migrations called                          
      2300 +     out; golden-frame and e2e suites gate releases.         
      2301 +   Deep dive: docs/19-deployment-and-release.md.             
      2302 +                                                             
      2303  -------------------------------------------------------------
            -----------------------------------

           -neering]

           +d Roadmap]

      2314 +     cockpit shell with chat + live terminal + control surfac
           +e + usage meter. EXIT: a fresh                               
      2315 +     Windows box can install core deps and hold a live Claude
           + session in the cockpit.

      2319 +     transcribe/detect/level/grade), and the reel pipeline as

      2320 +     reel" works end to end on the PoC clip, reproducibly, wi

      2321 +

           +e UX; EDD inspector/diff; incremental

           +k system; basic plugin loading.

           +nual tooling.                                                
      2325 +

           +les/transitions/templates; GPU paths                         
      2327 +     hardened; performance/regression suite; crash recovery; 
           +doctor; telemetry (opt-in).                                  
      2328 +     EXIT: external plugin authors ship; stability metrics me
           +et bar.

           +; full docs; golden-frame/e2e gates;                         
      2331 +     accessibility complete. EXIT: 1.0 release.              
      2332 +                                                             
      2333 +   Phase 6 - Plugin SDK maturity & ecosystem. Stable versione
           +d APIs; richer renderers (e.g.                               
      2334 +     HyperFrames signature-moment); look-system marketplace;

      2335 +                                                             
      2336 +   Phase 7 - Cloud rendering (opt-in). Offload heavy final re
           +nders to remote workers using the                            
      2337 +     content-addressed DAG; local cache authoritative; privac
           +y-preserving.                                                
      2338 +

      2340 +     editing (CRDT/merge on the AST).

           +===================================

           + --------------------------------------

      2364 +

           + Structured EDD + validation gates; QA/                      
      2370 +                                                             
           +  critique loop; eval harness; bounded                       
      2371 +                                                             
           +  autonomy

           + Prompt caching; cheap subagents;                            
      2373 +

           +  Tiered GPU enablement; faster-whisper;                     
      2375 +                                                             
           +  clear user trade-off (PoC F3)

           + Pin encoders/settings; tolerance-based                      
      2377 +
