      2392 + 28. OPEN QUESTIONS                                          
      2393 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2394 +                                                             
      2395 +   Q1  Daemon topology: Electron main vs a separate forked se
           +rvice for render durability - confirm                        
      2396 +       at Phase 1 (leaning forked service so a UI crash never
           + kills a render).                                            
      2397 +   Q2  EDD time model: pure seconds vs frame-exact rationals 
           +at the EDD level (IR will be                                 
      2398 +       frame-exact regardless) - decide in Phase 1.          
      2399 +   Q3  Caption word-timing source: distribute-within-segment 
           +vs a dedicated aligner (WhisperX) as                         
      2400 +       default - benchmark in Phase 2.                       
      2401 +   Q4  STYLE derivation: how far to push "make it feel like X
           +" (style transfer) vs explicit token                         
      2402 +       authoring - scope in Phase 3.                         
      2403 +   Q5  Cache scope: per-project only vs a shared global cache
           + by default - measure hit rates.                             
      2404 +   Q6  Plugin runtime isolation: worker threads vs a heavier 
           +VM/sandbox for untrusted code - decide                       
      2405 +       before the marketplace opens (Phase 4).               
      2406 +   Q7  Usage/limit surfacing fidelity: exactly what the CLI e
           +xposes vs estimation - validate against                      
      2407 +       the live CLI event stream.                            
      2408 +   Q8  Generative media policy: which (if any) providers ship
           + as first-party vs community-only.                           
      2409 +   Q9  HDR delivery: when to support HDR export vs SDR-only d
           +efault.                                                      
      2410 +   Q10 Multi-user EDD merge strategy (CRDT vs operational tra
           +nsform) - defer to Phase 8 but keep                          
      2411 +       the EDD merge-friendly now.                           
      2412 +   Deep dive: docs/21-risks-and-open-questions.md.           
      2413 +                                                             
      2414 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2415 + 29. TRADE-OFFS                                              
      2416 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2417 +                                                             
      2418 + The major trade-offs accepted, with rationale:              
      2419 +                                                             
      2420 +   29.1 Intent-first over timeline-first. We trade fine-grain
           +ed manual control for speed, reproducibility,                
      2421 +        and accessibility. Mitigated by the EDD inspector + l
           +anguage-driven fine adjustment; users                        
      2422 +        who want a manual GUI NLE are not the target (Non-goa
           +ls).                                                         
      2423 +                                                             
      2424 +   29.2 Spawn the Claude CLI over the Agent SDK. We trade som
           +e type-safety/in-process ergonomics for                      
      2425 +        the user's existing subscription auth (huge cost/adop
           +tion win) and full reuse of the CLI's                        
      2426 +        skills/MCP/plan-mode/usage. The SDK remains a documen
           +ted alternative (ADR-0002).                                  
      2427 +                                                             
      2428 +   29.3 Electron over Tauri. We trade binary size/RAM for eco
           +system maturity, media support, and 1:1                      
      2429 +        reuse of open-design's proven topology and our PoC's 
           +Windows validation (ADR-0001).                               
      2430 +                                                             
      2431 +   29.4 Cockpit-first over video-first v1. We trade an immedi
           +ately flashy demo for a reusable spine;                      
      2432 +        video ships as the first vertical so we still demonst
           +rate the wow (ADR-0003).                                     
      2433 +                                                             
      2434 +   29.5 Tiered install over fully-autonomous. We trade "every
           +thing ready instantly" for "no multi-GB                      
      2435 +        surprises and a fast first run"; heavy items install 
           +on first use with consent (ADR-0004).                        
      2436 +                                                             
      2437 +   29.6 Editing-as-compilation (EDD/IR/DAG) over direct tool 
           +scripting. We trade up-front                                 
      2438 +        architectural complexity for explainability, reproduc
           +ibility, incrementality, and caching -                       
      2439 +        the qualities that make the product trustworthy and f
           +ast (ADR-0005).                                              
      2440 +                                                             
      2441 +   29.7 Remotion + FFmpeg composite (with PNG-seq fallback) o
           +ver a single render engine. We trade a                       
      2442 +        more complex render path for robustness against the e
           +xact failure the PoC hit, and for the                        
      2443 +        best of both worlds (declarative graphics + determini
           +stic media) (ADR-0006).                                      
      2444 +                                                             
      2445 +   29.8 Windows-first over cross-platform day one. We trade i
           +mmediate Mac/Linux reach for matching                        
      2446 +        the user's machine and the validated PoC, shipping so
           +oner; cross-platform is a fast follow                        
      2447 +        (ADR-0007).                                          
      2448 +                                                             
      2449 +   29.9 Local-first over cloud-first. We trade managed-cloud 
           +convenience for privacy and offline                          
      2450 +        capability; cloud is opt-in and later (ADR-0008).    
      2451 +                                                             
      2452 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2453 + 30. ALTERNATIVE ARCHITECTURES (CONSIDERED AND COMPARED)     
      2454 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2455 +                                                             
      2456 + For each major decision, the viable alternatives, their pros
           +/cons, and why the chosen option wins.                       
      2457 + Full records in docs/adr/.                                  
      2458 +                                                             
      2459 + 30.1  Desktop shell                                         
      2460 +   A) Electron + Next.js [CHOSEN] - mature, rich media/Node e
           +cosystem, 1:1 with open-design,                              
      2461 +      PoC-validated on Windows. Con: heavier binaries/RAM.   
      2462 +   B) Tauri + Rust core - smaller/faster, modern; Con: diverg
           +es from open-design, fiddlier Windows                        
      2463 +      toolchain (WebView2/MSVC), smaller media ecosystem. Rec
           +onsider if footprint becomes critical.                       
      2464 +   C) Web + local daemon only - fastest to boot; Con: weak OS
           + integration (dialogs, GPU detect,                           
      2465 +      auto-update, tray). Useful as a dev/from-source mode (o
           +pen-design runs this way), not the                           
      2466 +      shipped product.                                       
      2467 +                                                             
      2468 + 30.2  Agent backbone                                        
      2469 +   A) Spawn Claude CLI headless [CHOSEN] - subscription auth,
           + full CLI feature reuse, literal to the                      
      2470 +      user's steer. Con: parse stream-json; CLI is a moving t
           +arget (mitigated by the adapter).                            
      2471 +   B) Claude Agent SDK (library) - type-safe, in-process; Con
           +: typically API-key billed (cost),                           
      2472 +      less "use what you already have". The documented altern
           +ative.                                                       
      2473 +   C) Agent-agnostic (any CLI: Claude/Codex/Cursor...) - max 
           +flexibility/OSS appeal; Con: largest                         
      2474 +      surface, hardest to make reliable. A possible later abs
           +traction.                                                    
      2475 +   D) Custom orchestration on the raw Messages API - maximum 
           +control; Con: rebuild the harness                            
      2476 +      (subagents/MCP/permissions/compaction) we get for free.
           + Rejected for v1.                                            
      2477 +                                                             
      2478 + 30.3  Edit representation                                   
      2479 +   A) Video AST / EDD + IR + DAG [CHOSEN] - explainable, repr
           +oducible, incremental, cacheable.                            
      2480 +      Con: up-front complexity.                              
      2481 +   B) Direct tool scripting (the PoC's mode) - simplest; Con:
           + not reproducible/inspectable/                               
      2482 +      incremental; no clean reasoning/execution boundary. Rej
           +ected as the product core.                                   
      2483 +   C) Adopt OpenTimelineIO as the native model - interoperabl
           +e; Con: heavier, NLE-centric, less                           
      2484 +      intent-bearing than our EDD. Consider as an import/expo
           +rt format, not the internal AST.                             
      2485 +                                                             
      2486 + 30.4  Render engine                                         
      2487 +   A) Remotion + FFmpeg composite, native-or-PNG-seq fallback
           + [CHOSEN] - declarative graphics +                           
      2488 +      deterministic media + robustness. Con: two substrates. 
      2489 +   B) FFmpeg-only (drawtext/overlay filters) - one tool; Con:
           + weak for rich motion graphics/word-                         
      2490 +      level caption animation; PoC showed drawtext font/compl
           +exity pain. Insufficient alone.                              
      2491 +   C) Remotion-only (native) - one declarative engine; Con: t
           +he native compositor failed in the                           
      2492 +      PoC; encoding everything in React is heavy for raw medi
           +a ops. Insufficient alone.                                   
      2493 +   D) HyperFrames (HTML/CSS/GSAP -> MP4) as the engine - stro
           +ng for captions; Con: cut-sensitive,                         
      2494 +      narrower; better as an optional renderer plugin.       
      2495 +                                                             
      2496 + 30.5  Installation strategy                                 
      2497 +   A) Tiered (core auto, heavy on-demand) [CHOSEN] - balance.
           + B) Fully autonomous (install all up                         
      2498 +   front) - zero-config but big first download. C) Ask-before
           +-each - max control, most friction.                          
      2499 +   (A) chosen; (B)/(C) selectable as user preferences.       
      2500 +                                                             
      2501 + 30.6  Concurrency/topology                                  
      2502 +   A) Single privileged daemon + sandboxed renderer [CHOSEN] 
           +- security + open-design parity.                             
      2503 +   B) Privileged renderer (nodeIntegration) - simpler; Con: u
           +nacceptable blast radius. Rejected.                          
      2504 +                                                             
      2505 + 30.7  Platform                                              
      2506 +   A) Windows-first [CHOSEN]. B) Cross-platform day one - cle
           +aner abstractions, slower v1.                                
      2507 +   C) Windows+macOS - middle ground. (A) chosen for speed and
           + PoC alignment.                                              
      2508 +                                                             
      2509 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2510 + 31. DECISION RECORDS (SUMMARY)                              
      2511 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2512 +                                                             
      2513 + Full ADRs (context, options, decision, consequences) live in
           + docs/adr/. Summary:                                         
      2514 +                                                             
      2515 +   ADR-0001  Electron + Next.js desktop shell.            Sta
           +tus: Accepted.                                               
      2516 +   ADR-0002  Spawn the Claude CLI headless as backbone.   Sta
           +tus: Accepted. (Agent SDK = alt.)                            
      2517 +   ADR-0003  Agentic cockpit first; video = first vertical. S
           +tatus: Accepted.                                             
      2518 +   ADR-0004  Tiered installation (core auto / heavy on-demand
           +). Status: Accepted.                                         
      2519 +   ADR-0005  Video AST/EDD + IR + execution DAG (editing-as-c
           +ompilation). Status: Accepted.                               
      2520 +   ADR-0006  Remotion + FFmpeg composite with PNG-sequence fa
           +llback. Status: Accepted.                                    
      2521 +   ADR-0007  Windows-first; macOS/Linux later.            Sta
           +tus: Accepted.                                               
      2522 +   ADR-0008  Local-first; daemon sole privileged process; SSR
           +F-guarded proxy. Status: Accepted.                           
      2523 +                                                             
      2524 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2525 + 32. APPENDICES                                              
      2526 +=============================================================
           +===================================                          
      2527 +                                                             
      2528 + The following references support implementation. Full conten
           +t lives under docs/appendices/.                              
      2529 +                                                             
      2530 +   Appendix A - Glossary (docs/appendices/A-glossary.md)     
      2531 +     EDD, Video AST, IR, execution DAG, cockpit, daemon, the 
           +CLI, MCP, STYLE.md, proxy, golden                            
      2532 +     frame, content-addressed cache, tonemap, LUFS, NVENC, pl
           +an/auto mode, look system, etc.                              
      2533 +                                                             
      2534 +   Appendix B - FFmpeg recipes from the proof-of-concept (doc
           +s/appendices/B-ffmpeg-recipes.md)                            
      2535 +     The exact, proven invocations: two-pass loudnorm to -14 
           +LUFS + afftdn denoise; HLG->Rec.709                          
      2536 +     SDR tonemap + light grade (zscale/tonemap); alternating 
           +"breathe" punch-in zoom expression;                          
      2537 +     scene/frame-diff cut detection; silencedetect smart-cut;
           + PNG-sequence overlay + composite +                          
      2538 +     mux; platform-optimized H.264/AAC export. These are the 
           +canonical specs the typed FFmpeg tool                        
      2539 +     constructs.                                             
      2540 +                                                             
      2541 +   Appendix C - Claude CLI event protocol & adapter contract 
           +(docs/appendices/C-claude-cli-event-protocol.md)             
      2542 +     The spawn invocation; the stream-json event types consum
           +ed (thinking, tool_use, tool_result,

  your PoC ¬∑ C the Claude CLI event protocol ¬∑ D the JSON schema reference

  The architecture in one breath

  OpenVideo ‚ÄĒ local-first, intent-first. An Electron + Next.js cockpit over one
  privileged Node daemon that spawns the Claude CLI headless (your Pro
  subscription, no API bill) as the reasoning brain and
  FFmpeg/Whisper/Remotion/yt-dlp as deterministic tools. Every edit is a Video 
  AST (EDD) ‚Üí IR ‚Üí execution DAG ‚Üí render ‚ÄĒ explainable, versioned,
  incrementally cached. v1 = the agentic cockpit, with the proven reel pipeline
  as the first pluggable vertical. Tiered installer, Windows-first.

  All eight locked decisions (Electron, Claude-CLI-spawn, cockpit-first, tiered
  install, Video-AST/IR, Remotion+PNG-seq+FFmpeg, Windows-first, local-first)
  are reflected consistently across the PRD and ADRs.

  PRODUCT_REQUIREMENTS_DOCUMENT.txt top-to-bottom, then docs/00-INDEX.md for the
  deep dives.

‚óŹ Write(packages\project\src\probe.ts)
  ‚éŅ ¬†Wrote 36 lines to packages\project\src\probe.ts
       1 /** OpenVideo ‚ÄĒ media probing via ffprobe (PRD ¬ß11.2 INGEST). */
       2 
       3 import { runFfprobe } from "@openvideo/render";
       4 import type { Probe } from "@openvideo/edd";
       5 
       6 function fps(rate: string | undefined): number {
       7   if (!rate) return 30;
       8   const [n, d] = rate.split("/").map(Number);
       9   return d ? Math.round((n! / d) * 1000) / 1000 : (n ?? 30);
      10 }

‚óŹ Good ‚ÄĒ that surfaced a real bug: the machine has an NVIDIA GPU, so the encoder
  is h264_nvenc, but ultrafast is an x264-only preset and NVENC rejects it. The
  preset must be encoder-specific. (Note the export still verified 540√ó960
  H.264 ‚ÄĒ that was the demo-render output from the earlier instance; the project
  render genuinely failed.) Let me fix the preset to be encoder-aware.

‚óŹ Update(packages\render\src\ffmpeg.ts)
  ‚éŅ ¬†Added 11 lines, removed 2 lines
      25    input_thresh: string;
      26  }
      27  
      28 -/** x264/NVENC preset. Default "slow" for final quality; overri
         -de to "ultrafast" for fast previews. */                        
      29 -const PRESET = process.env.OPENVIDEO_PRESET ?? "slow";         
      28 +/**                                                            
      29 + * Encoder-specific preset. OPENVIDEO_PRESET is a *speed tier* 
         +("fast" | "final", default "final").                           
      30 + * libx264 uses ultrafast..slow; NVENC uses named presets (fast
         +/slow) ‚ÄĒ "ultrafast" is x264-only and                          
      31 + * errors on NVENC, so the tier is mapped per encoder.         
      32 + */                                                            
      33 +function presetFor(encoder: string): string {                  
      34 +  const tier = (process.env.OPENVIDEO_PRESET ?? "final").toLowe
         +rCase();                                                       
      35 +  const fast = tier === "fast" || tier === "ultrafast" || tier 
         +=== "preview";                                                 
      36 +  if (encoder === "h264_nvenc" || encoder === "hevc_nvenc") ret
         +urn fast ? "fast" : "slow";                                    
      37 +  return fast ? "ultrafast" : "slow"; // libx264               
      38 +}                                                              
      39  
      40  const resolve0 = (ctx: ToolContext, node: DAGNode): string => c
          tx.resolveInput(node.inputs[0] ?? "");
      41

‚óŹ Background command "Restart daemon with PRD-prompt routes" failed with exit code 1

‚óŹ The daemon crashed (exit 1) ‚ÄĒ root cause is a real robustness bug: when a
  client disconnects mid‚ÄĎstream (my curl --max-time 3 cut the connection), the
  SSE loop kept calling res.write on a closed socket, which threw and took the
  process down. That must never crash a long‚ÄĎrunning daemon. Let me harden the
  SSE channel (guard writes, detect disconnect, stop streaming) and add
  process‚ÄĎlevel safety nets.

     ---
     PART A ‚ÄĒ Design language & brand (jet-black, agency-grade)

     Two scopes, both token-driven (keep distinct): (1) the app's own UI design 
     system; (2) the
     project STYLE.md that constrains rendered video output (already documented
     ‚ÄĒ extend, don't replace).

     A1. Color ‚ÄĒ "Obsidian" jet-black system

     - True near-black base ramp (e.g. #050506 ‚Üí #0A0B0D ‚Üí #0E0F12 ‚Üí #16181D ‚Üí 
     #1E2127), not navy. The
     earlier navy #0E1C2B becomes an accent-surface, not the base. Jet-black
     canvas, layered
     graphite panels, hairline borders (rgba(255,255,255,0.06‚Äď0.12)).
     - One restrained metallic accent (warm gold #C9A227 / #E7C766) for primary
     actions & emphasis;
     semantic colors (success/warn/error/info) tuned for dark; a small set of
     editorial accent hues for
     category chips (fonts, b-roll, music, images, VFX).
     - Full token ramp with light-on-dark contrast ‚Č• WCAG AA; an optional light
     theme later.

     A2. Typography ‚ÄĒ maximised, Google-Fonts-linked

     - App UI type system: a confident editorial pairing ‚ÄĒ a grotesk/display for
     headings + a highly
     legible UI sans for body + a mono for the terminal/EDD. Curated, licensed,
     self-hosted via
     @fontsource (offline-safe).
     - Project/output fonts = the live Google Fonts catalog (the user's explicit
     ask). A Font
     Studio panel: searchable, filterable (serif/sans/display/mono/handwriting,
     weights, language
     subsets), live preview on the user's own caption text, favorites, pairing
     suggestions. Fonts fetch
     keyless on-demand via the Google Fonts CSS2 endpoint / @fontsource
     packages; a curated
     "starter" set ships bundled. Selected fonts resolve into STYLE.md
     caption/typography tokens and the
     Remotion caption components.
     - A real type scale (modular), weights, tracking, optical sizes; editorial
     display sizes for the
     Home/empty states.

     A3. Spacing, grid, elevation, radius, motion, icons

     - 4/8px spacing scale; a studio grid (left rail ¬∑ main ¬∑ right inspector ¬∑
     bottom transport).
     - Elevation by surface tint + hairline + soft shadow (dark-tuned).
     Consistent radii.
     - Motion language: purposeful, fast, never gratuitous ‚ÄĒ Framer Motion for
     UI transitions, GSAP
     for the "alive" moments (terminal stream, render progress, library hovers).
     Respect
     prefers-reduced-motion.
     - Icon set: a single consistent line-icon family (e.g. Lucide), plus custom
     marks for the editing
     primitives (cut, grade, caption, b-roll, VFX, voiceover-later).

     A4. Component library (shadcn/ui + custom studio components)

     Buttons, inputs, selects, sliders, tabs, dialogs, popovers, tooltips,
     toasts, command palette
     (cmdk), resizable panels, context menus, data tables, cards, chips,
     segmented controls, progress,
     scrubber/timeline primitives, waveform, color-grade controls, asset cards,
     drag-drop zones.

     A5. Brand kit system (per project)

     A Brand Kit surface: logo/handle, palette, fonts, caption style, motion
     amplitude, audio
     targets, b-roll/music policy ‚ÄĒ editable in the UI, persisted into the
     project STYLE.md, reused across
     edits. "Derive from reference" (e.g. make it feel like MagnatesMedia)
     proposes a kit.

     PART B ‚ÄĒ Information architecture & screens (two-mode UX)

     Every surface supports Auto mode ("drop + one-liner, leave it to the app")
     and Manual control
     ("do it all and control it"). Plan/auto + permissions already exist in the
     protocol; the UI exposes

     - Top bar: project switcher ¬∑ global search/command-palette (‚ĆėK) ¬∑
     model/effort/mode controls ¬∑
     usage+limits meter ¬∑ render-queue indicator ¬∑ settings.
     - Left rail (collapsible): Projects ¬∑ Assets ¬∑ Library ¬∑ Brand Kit ¬∑
     Agents/Skills ¬∑ Plugins ¬∑
     Render Queue ¬∑ Settings/Doctor.
     - Main + right inspector + bottom transport depending on the active screen.

     B2. Screens (each gets an ASCII wireframe + states in docs)

     1. Home / Projects ‚ÄĒ editorial empty state; "New project / Drop a clip /
     Paste a brief"; recent
     projects as premium cards (thumbnail, platform, duration, last render).
     2. The Studio (main editor) ‚ÄĒ the heart:
       - Left: chat (intent) + the "alive" terminal (two layers: friendly +
     raw).
       - Center: Preview (sandboxed) with transport/scrubber; toggle to
     Timeline/EDD view (the
     generated timeline ‚ÄĒ tracks: a-roll, captions, graphics, b-roll,
     audio/music/SFX, VFX), with
     inline EDD node inspection + provenance + diff.
       - Right: contextual Inspector (selected clip/caption/graphic/grade/audio)
     with full manual
     controls ‚ÄĒ the "control it" surface.
       - Bottom: transport, render/preview/export, plan-approval bar.
       - Plan mode: the blueprint renders as an approvable, editable proposal;
     Auto mode: runs
     end-to-end, pausing only on gated actions.
     3. Library browser ‚ÄĒ tabs: Fonts (Google Fonts) ¬∑ B-roll ¬∑
     Music/Discography ¬∑
     SFX ¬∑ AI Images ¬∑ Templates/Looks. Browse, preview (hover-play video, audio
     scrub,
     live font preview), license badge, insert-into-timeline / set-as-style,
     override.
     4. Brand Kit / STYLE editor ‚ÄĒ visual editor over STYLE.md (palette, fonts,
     caption style, motion,
     audio targets, anti-patterns); live preview; "derive from reference".
     5. Color ‚ÄĒ grade controls (tonemap toggle, WB, contrast curve, vibrance,
     sharpen, vignette),
     before/after, scopes-later.
     6. Audio mixer ‚ÄĒ voice chain, loudness target (-14 LUFS default + meter),
     music bed + ducking,
     SFX cues on a small timeline.
     7. Caption studio ‚ÄĒ word-level caption styling, emphasis terms, karaoke
     preview, language/
     romanization, safe-margins, font from Font Studio.
     8. VFX panel ‚ÄĒ object removal (VOID): select/track a region, preview,
     apply; tiered-install
     gated; heavy-job progress.
     9. Footage analysis panel ‚ÄĒ claude-video: the agent's visual read of the
     footage (keyframes,
     shot list, what's on screen) feeding smarter planning.
     10. Render Queue ‚ÄĒ jobs, phases, ETA, cache hits, cancel, outputs;
     notifications.
     11. Settings / Installer / Doctor ‚ÄĒ hardware profile, tiered install with
     sizes+consent,
     repair/rollback, keystore for provider/API keys, model/effort defaults,
     theme.
     12. Usage ‚ÄĒ session token/cost + plan-limit progress + "approaching limit"
     warning.

     B3. Cross-cutting UX

     - Command palette (‚ĆėK) for everything; full keyboard map; accessibility (SR
     labels, focus,
     reduced-motion, scalable type); responsive down to a laptop; toasts + a
     notification center.

     ---
     PART C ‚ÄĒ Library & provider system (packages/library)

     A typed provider registry so b-roll/music/SFX/font/image sources are
     pluggable (open-design
     plugin sensibility). Each provider declares: id, kind, auth (none |
     apiKey), license, capabilities,
     search/fetch/preview methods.

     - Kinds: font ¬∑ broll ¬∑ music ¬∑ sfx ¬∑ image ¬∑ template/look.
     - Keyless now: Google Fonts (font) ¬∑ generated/vector b-roll (Remotion) ¬∑
     bundled royalty-free
     SFX + music starter set ¬∑ local AI-image (only if a model is present).
     - Key-gated wired-inactive: Pexels/Pixabay (broll/image) ¬∑ Freesound (sfx)
     ¬∑ Free Music Archive/
     others (music) ¬∑ hosted image APIs ‚ÄĒ read keys from the encrypted keystore;
     show "add key to
     enable" until present. Never scrape; every result carries a license badge
     (PRD ¬ß4.3).
     - Caching + licensing: downloaded/previewed assets cached content-addressed
     under the project;
     license + attribution stored with the asset manifest entry.
     - EDD/data-model additions: b-roll-from-provider asset refs,
     generated-image assets, font refs on
     caption/typography, a music/score track + SFX cues (extend existing audio
     track), provenance for
     provider/license. (Update packages/edd + Appendix D.)
     - Agent: a Library/Curator agent + MCP tools (library.search,
     library.preview,
     library.insert) so the Director can pull on-brand, copyright-safe assets
     automatically ‚ÄĒ or the
     user picks manually.

     ---
     PART D ‚ÄĒ External model integrations NOW (packages/integrations)

     Typed adapters + MCP tools + tiered install. Two now; three deferred.

     D1. claude-video ‚ÄĒ footage vision-analysis (light; build fully now)

     - Pipeline (we already have the deps): ffmpeg extracts keyframes at an
     adaptive rate + whisper
     transcript ‚Üí frames+timestamps sent to Claude (vision) ‚Üí a structured
     shot/„Äčscene analysis
     (what's on screen, shot types, energy, on-screen text, dead/usable ranges).
     - Surfaces: the Footage analysis panel; feeds the Planner/Story/Hook/B-roll
     agents for
     genuinely footage-aware edits (today they only see transcript+probe). MCP
     tool analyze_footage.
     - Adapter wraps the logic in our own code (MIT-licensed approach); no heavy
     download.

     D2. VOID ‚ÄĒ interaction-aware object removal (heavy; adapter + tiered 
     install)

     - Capability: remove a person/logo/object from a shot with realistic
     physics/shadow cleanup.
     - Adapter + MCP tool vfx_remove_object (inputs: video + mask/region +
     prompt). Heavy tier:
     CogVideoX/SAM weights download on first use with consent (Installation
     Agent); GPU-bound; CPU path
     flagged as impractical. Apache-2.0.
     - Surfaces: the VFX panel (region select ‚Üí preview ‚Üí apply); a VFX agent
     the Director can
     delegate to ("remove the photobomber at 0:12").

     D3. Deferred (documented as roadmap only, NOT built now)

     - chandra (OCR/doc‚Üístructured) ‚ÄĒ for future faceless-explainer/document
     ingest.
     - voicebox (MCP-native voice studio) + VoxCPM (TTS/voice clone) ‚ÄĒ future
     voiceover/dubbing.
     Note voicebox is MCP-native, so later it slots in as an MCP server with
     minimal glue.

     D4. New agents (extend docs/05 + packages/agents)

     Footage-Analysis (Vision) agent ¬∑ VFX/Object-removal agent ¬∑
     Library/Curator agent ¬∑ Image-gen agent
     (keyless/local now, hosted later). Each with the standard spec
     (remit/inputs/outputs/tools/perm/
     failure/effort). All heavy/networked actions are gated MCP tools (CLAUDE.md
     invariant 5).

     ---
     PART E ‚ÄĒ Daemon additions

     Extend apps/daemon (zero-dep node:http + SSE, already hardened against
     client-disconnect):
     - GET /api/library/:kind/search ¬∑ GET /api/library/preview ¬∑ POST 
     /api/projects/:id/library/insert
     - POST /api/projects/:id/analyze (claude-video footage analysis, SSE)
     - POST /api/projects/:id/vfx/remove-object (VOID, SSE, tiered-install
     gated)
     - GET /api/fonts/search + on-demand font fetch; POST /api/images/generate
     (if local model present)
     - keystore endpoints for provider keys (write-only, encrypted). Reuse
     existing patterns; keep the
     daemon the sole privileged process (ADR-0008).
     - Important: the new Next.js cockpit consumes these over the same protocol;
     CORS/loopback + token
     guard; the daemon may serve the built Next app in production and proxy in
     dev.
